=== Saturday January 31, 2004 ===

I Dream of Freedom

Something that I have spoken of in the past is how I used to dream.  I have vivid dreams, plot driven and crisp, even now... however, when I was younger, I also had full control of every aspect.  Well, at the very least, I always knew that I was dreaming and would lucidly explore my surroundings and my control over them.  Along the path of growing up I somehow lost that control.  I lost that absolute lucidity in my dreams.  Now I'm almost always myself, but altered to fit the dream.  A character, or many characters in my own subconscious' plots and devices.

I know that there are ways to gain that lucidity again.  I think that's something I'm going to be looking at.  Maybe it's because I am very time conscious.  I don't like to think of wasted time.  Or time where I wasn't in control of myself.  Then again... some of the dreams go in directions I'd never have consciously thought.  Adventures.

I may not be as caught up in my dreams as I used to be.  When I was younger, I used to look forward to bedtime... or at least the part that happend after I got to sleep.  At that time, my punishment for not doing all of my grade 1 work at school, or for anything else at that matter, was to go to bed right after dinner.  Every night.  It's actually one of my stronger memories.  My weeknight straight to bed nights.  But... I guess I didn't care in the end.  My dreams were just more time to be concious as far as I was concerned.  I'd wake up and sometimes I'd start out in my apartment... but different.  I'd blink, and I'd be somewhere else.  My Grandmother's house was a big place I'd end up.  I still have dreams that take place in that old house.  Always that house, but different.  Larger than life.  More expansive, larger rooms, but undeniably my grandmother's house.

It's how I was able to visit Australia long after returning here to Canada.  I'd have dreams of the Beach Road we used to live on, and I'd know people living along there.  Of course, as everything, it was the same 'essence' of the place, similar shape, but largely altered.  Everything seemed larger, more expansive, kind of like looking through a door peephole.  Except without visual distortion.

Another place my dreams often take me are my Grandparent's old cottage.  Except, often the body of water it's attached to is different.  Sometimes the Ocean, sometimes a lake, somemtimes a large river.  Rapids.  Sometimes there are many other buildings near, other times just forest.

It's often twilight or dawn in my dreams.  Twilight is my favourite time.  When the trees don't cast shadows, but stand as tall sillhouettes, shadows themselves against a darkly bright sky.  Where you can see their faces peering at you with their ancient wisdom.  Their limbs grasping at the failing light, but firmly rooted where they stand.

I also often dream of houses.  Rooms, many rooms, passages, elevators, apartments.  Air ducts, closed spaces.  One room is always connected somehow to another.  Sometimes, it's just hard to find.  In one dream, to escape something I had to push through glass in the dream.  I pushed up against the window and slowly, like thick jellow, I pushed through.  It felt like when you're in a bathtub and you pull the plug, and still lie there.  As the water drains you feel it's edge against you, sinking as crawls down  your skin.  I love that feeling, slowly feeling the weight of the world catch up to you.  No longer weightless.  Waking up from dreams is like that.

It's hard to believe, to coceive, that the people in my dreams.  Their characterization, their appearance, their personality, everything comes from somewhere.  It always strikes me as incredible.  Dreams... I tell ya, they intruige me to no end.

Bloody amazing is what they are.  That we have the ability to create entire worlds.  Visual, tactile, alive.  Within our own minds.  While we're just lying there.  The mind, what a powerful thing.

And now, so that my brain gets a little more oxygen, I'm going to the mall to get a haircut.  I've been depriving a floor of my hair somewhere.  I think I should get on it.

Ciao for now,

Shane

[Posted 1/31/2004 at 10:59 AM]

My roommate Thomas says that you can learn to lucid dream.  He says that the way he's done it is to stop at various points in the day and say to himself, "am I dreaming?"  He takes in his surroundings and notes that he is very much awake.  But, he says if he makes this a habit, he starts to do it in his dreams too.  And then he'll notice that it isn't quite reality and he'll be lucid dreaming.  I couldn't ever remember enough during the day to make it a habit.

=== Friday January 30, 2004 ===

Music and Ecstacy

Let me talk a little bit today about music.  I began my love of music with a blue Texas Instrument product I forget the name of.  Something like a basic tiny, one or two octave electric keyboard/music playfield.  I kept it, and used it for many yeas. Until, in the end, all that could be heard were unmusical blips and squeeks.  It's where I got my ear for music.  Halftones, patterns, songs.  It had a feature to listen and then copy what you heard.  It would start with one note, then add one note more each time.  It was my favourite game.

As I grew I started up in piano lessons, got to around grade 5 in piano and then my interest in piano tapered off.  My interest in music never did.  In High school I started into the musicals in grade 11, took a vocal class, and then moved on to University for Computer Science.  I didn't take any courses in music, unfortunately, but I did steal away into the soundproof rooms they had for music practice.  I'd have my lyrics in hand, and I'd sing.  And I'd sing.

I still sing, when the house is empty and nobody is around.  But, singing makes me feel alive.  And hearing beautiful harmony always always always gives me goosebumps.  Evanescence is one of those bands who give me goosebumps.  Sometimes I'll drift to sleep listening to that voice, and that music, and that atmosphere.  And, as I spoke of the sadness, there's joy as well.  The music washes over me and I begin to remember.  I remember life that's gone by, the things that never finished, the good and the bad.  And there's the music!  And I smile because despite my sadness the music stirrs up, my body goosebumps all over.  It's like I drift otuside my own skin and float.

That music, and other music like it just always gets me.  It's bitter-sweetness makes me feel more alive than I ever knew.  I almost lose myself.

It's wonderful.

So music is something that is always going to be a part of my life.  Whether it takes center stage or not is something of a question for the future.  For now, I sing my secret songs and listen to harmony whenever I can.  It's hauntingly beautiful.

It's beautifully haunting. ;-)

And music can move emotion so well.  It brings us places we've almost forgotten.  It takes us back and makes us smile, and makes us cry.

Happy Friday!

Shane

[Posted 1/30/2004 at 8:39 AM]

=== Wednesday January 28, 2004 ===

Lately at Night

For a little while now I find myself melancholy at night.  I find myself, however, embracing the melancholy.  I am the kind of person who does feel emotion fairly strongly, however, for most people I only ever show certain emotions.  I was thinking about this today.

In Public I seem to show either happiness, anger (distaste) or apathy.  I thought deeper about this.  I don't like people seeing me sad.  Sadness is almost exclusively my secret emotion.  At least, physically.  I'm fairly free with it in writing,  here, where things are distant and so are the people reading.  At night, I intentionally put on dark and brooding music to get myself in that melancholy state.  My alone time, when I get to enjoy just thinking about some of the things that aren't working or haven't worked in my life.

I don't know if it's related, but most mornings I wake up in good spirits.  My days usually see me go through cycles like that.  I admit to being an emotional person, but very few people will ever see tears running down my face.  I find it odd.  I've always thought of myself as openly emotional... but knowing that I feel emotion and showing others all of them is another thing altogether.

But, why then is the stigma of being emotional in public attached with the tears and the sad.  Why do I find no problem feeling anger or happiness?  Anger, I think, is the easy answer.  For me, anger is reflex.  Instinct.  If I get cut off by a car my face shows my anger, you could almost hear me growl.  My desire to kick the car is great.  Joy, is also kind of reflex.  When something happens that makes us smile, it's almost instant.  No thought required.  Most of the time.  With sadness though, for me at least, it usually involves thought.  Either through thinking from other points of view, or just thinking and mulling over my own life.  It's this act of thinking that draws it into hiding.  I can control it more than apathy, anger or happiness.

I'm not sure, but that might be the key for me.  I don't know.  Just the entire emotional process was on my mind today as I made my way to work.  Reflex, and then thought.  Controlling the reflex.  Reacting contrary to reflex.

Food for thought, and now to bed.  Going to grab some quality thinking time before I get to sleep, put on some Evenescence and drift away.

...gimme the beat boys, sooth my soul...

Sweet Dreams

Shane

[Posted 1/28/2004 at 9:15 PM]

=== Monday January 26, 2004 ===

Mel
In Loving Memory

I know there are many out there right now that have gone through and are currently going through dealing with the loss of a loved one.  I hear about death every day.  In the news, in stories, from friends and family.  I hear about death, and it never really hits me.  It makes me stop and think for a little bit about how hard it must be.  I've been through death in the past.  My Godfather, my Cousin, my Aunt, Grandfather, and the list goes on.  I'm no stranger to loss of life, and yet, the most recent event in my own life is affecting me a great deal.

When I was 17 I went to France with a youth group.  I met many people during this trip, and grew closer to people I had only slightly known before then.  Mel was one of those people.  She was engaged at the time I met her, and I liked the guy, so it's not exactly like I had a chance at anything but friendship... and that was more than enough.  Mel was the kind of person who smiled often, had a good sense of humour, and cared a great deal about people.  After we came back from france, I went over to her and her family's house a few times.  Halloween for pumpkin carving, and just hanging out.

In all honesty, I was a very shy person socially, and what friendship we had faded as I moved forward in my life, and out of town.  I told her that I'd give her a call when I developed my pictures from France.  I developed them three years later, and didn't have the nerve to call her and her family out of the blue.

She was a great person, a beautiful person, and I've recently found out that around Christmas this past year, she passed away.

The other week I found out and it just hit me.  She is gone.  And I don't know why it's bothering me as much as it is.  I spent some time this past weekend imagining that she might be able to see me, and went through my pictures from France, desperately trying to keep a promise long since passed.

Mel is gone, but her spirit lives on in the people who knew her even a little bit, as I did.  I know that if she could impact me as much as she did for as small a friendship we had, then there are very many people in the world that feel the loss.

I'm sorry for the sad post.  I've just been going through different stages, and I'm not familiar with this.

I wish all of you life and love.  Especially love, the love of friends, family, and that one person who brings even more meaning to your life than you ever knew possible.  They all make us bigger and stronger.  They all make us a little more than we were.  And they all stay with us, no matter how much time passes, and no matter how much distance.

For sharing even part of her life, I thank her for the memories.

Peace,

Shane

[Posted 1/26/2004 at 10:44 PM]

=== Tuesday January 20, 2004 ===

[IMAGE: http://i.xanga.com/Stultiloquent/hick-whoppers.jpg]

Almost frighteningly at peace...

This morning sometime before my alarm sounded and after I awoke I had an identity crisis.  I didn't know who I was, I didn't know where I was, and I didn't know what day of the week it was.  I didn't know what end of the bed I was lying at, and I didn't know why I was.

It scared the hell out of me.  For those seconds or minutes (hard to tell in times like that) I was without idenity.  I've never been without identity before.  In fact, it's one of my greatest fears, to lose the identity that is me.  It's a fear, I realize, that will never truly affect me after the fact... lol, so I guess I shouldn't worry too much about it.  But it's true affectation is the possibility of it happening.

At the same time that it was scaring the hell out of me, well, not at the same time.  Just after I found myself again.  I actually liked the sensation of having lost myself a little bit in those moments.  Firstly, I think it had something to do with me probably having a great sleep.  Also, I'm sleeping on the wrong side of the bed, because lately I'm falling asleep to music, and the speakers are at the end of the bed.  Thirdly, the pre-alarm that I have set is a cd set to play 30 minutes before my alarm.  To bring me out of sleep slowly.

It's entitled:

Ritual Music of the Tibetan Monks - Mantras for Meditation.

It's melodic, rhythmic, earthy, peaceful, and wonderful to crawl from sleep to.  Helps me remember my dreams when I crawl from sleep that way.  Slowly and in stages.  More specifically, I listen in t he morning to the first part of "Netten Chudruk", the one meditation that exists on CD2.

Ironically, in the panic of this morning, I forgot my dreams of last night.  Well, bring on the night, and the midnight hour.  These 40 winks are going to be great.  And I'll let you all know what happens tomorrow.

Sleep well, but maybe not so well that you completely forget yourself.  Though I'm telling you, it's kind of refreshing... but after the fact.

Shane

=== Monday January 19, 2004 ===

you fringe me like no other
tattered blue, but beautiful
stonewashed, denim godess

sink  into me, or sink with me
i could drown, you on my arm
the earth could wash us clean

and all for just a word,
a feeling when you slip, wet,
recovered from that yesterday

a neon sun, and bliss
without the caring of heartache
before the turning of the clock

shane

=== Wednesday January 14, 2004 ===

Different

You lie awake at night.  (You know who you are).  You lie awake at night and wonder how it came to this.  The same old thing, the same old week, the same old year.  You wonder how you slipped so far from your truest hopes and most heartfelt dreams.  How the tomorrow you had envisioned is now the yesterday that never happened.  You see the stars, and all you see are stars.  You close your eyes, and all you see is darkness.

You lie awake at night, and wonder how one year turned into 20, and all the things you worked for are the same things you slowly drove away... day by day.  You lie awake and ponder why it happened, and you begin to think it has to change.  You begin to feel as though the cage isn't so small.  You begin to perhaps see the way through the bars.  And at about 5 minutes to sleep you realize that it WILL change.  Tomorrow.  Tomorrow you'll put it all down on paper, and begin planning your change of life.  Begin finally living the way you always wanted to.  You'll leave the grind behind and pick up your passion.

You lie awake at night, and suddenly get tired, knowing that it's going to be okay.  Tomorrow.  And the darkness doesn't seem so dim.

But

When you wake up, you remember the thoughts but forget the passions that drove them.  You remember the feelings but forget the why.  You realize you must have been dilerious so late at night.  You weren't thinking right.  You go to work and come  home tired, food for the table, and you go to bed.

I lie awake at night...

[Posted 1/14/2004 at 10:31 PM]

=== Wednesday January 14, 2004 ===

Turtle (Part II) read Part I below if you want this to make sense...

He now knew what alone meant.  He hadn’t known what alone was before, because he had no reason to feel any different than he always had.  He knew now, though, that if Light were to go away, he would feel alone.  So, now, he knew that he must not be alone.  Following that thought, he just continued to be, and watched Light and Dark exist all around him.  They would change places often.  First there would be Light, and then Dark.  Then there would be Dark and then Light.

As was Turtle’s pattern, however, he soon began to think about different things.  Light and Dark began to be the same over and over again.  They would change places, and that would be it.  Dark and Light changing all around him constantly.  He couldn’t keep track of them both.  He began to get confused even when he wasn’t thinking.  It was too chaotic.  Too unorganized.  He knew that his thoughts were clearer to him than Light and Dark were to his senses.  It bothered him that he couldn’t follow the patterns that Light and Dark would take across his perception.  It bothered him and he almost. Almost. Wished that there was either only Light or only Dark.  Except before that thought developed to the point of a desire, he realized that he might miss one in its absence.  So he kept thinking on how it might be different.

Turtle soon thought that if Light and Dark were a little separate, things might be different.  That perhaps, if they followed a better pattern, things might be clearer to him.  And, to his increasing amazement, it was so.  Light and Dark became separate from each other.  Now there was Light, there was Dark, and there was the time between Light and Dark where everything around him seemed made of both Light and Dark.

This is perfect! Turtle thought to himself.  This is exactly what I wanted!  And again, he would have smiled, but still didn’t have anything to smile with.  New thoughts started to form within him.  He thought about time again, and found himself thinking about when the next Dark would come, or the next Light, and began to realize that he could keep track of the passing of time a little better than he used to be able to.  Why, only three Dark’s ago, I was thinking about feeling the Light and Dark.  And next Dark, I want to think a little more about the time between Light and Dark.  So, in this way, he became more aware of the passage of time.

Turtle was happy for a time.  A thousand Dark’s and a thousand Light’s passed by in the same way.  And Turtle thought.  He thought so hard and kept thinking about things even when they started to confuse him.  Turtle wondered what had made the Light and the Dark.  He knew that the Dark was always there.  Except he used to call it the Nothing.  And he figured he always existed, because he didn’t remember not existing.  And time was so hard to keep track of back when there was only Nothing.  So, he had always existed, but now he was existing with a capital E!

He began to think more on feeling.  The Light and the Dark seemed to be intangible.  They just were, like him.  They didn’t have a shape, or a form.  They were either there, or the other was, or they were blending from one to the other.  He began wanting more.  Change.  He had the patterns that he had previously desired.  Now he was getting bored with the pattern.  Over and over.  Light in and Dark out.  Same old, same old.  He wanted something absolutely and totally different.  Something solid.  Something with form.  Something to exist with him in the Light and in the Dark.

The only problem he saw with this, was that he had never known of anything solid.  There was the Light and Dark, and he couldn’t ‘feel’ them any more than he could ‘feel’ himself.  He could just see them, or not see them as the case may be.  If only there was something else existing here with me. Something hard, and something soft. No sooner had the thought crossed him, and there it was.  Something hard and something soft.  All around him on one side was something hard, and all around him on the other was something soft.  AND, he started thinking about how it seemed an interesting coincidence that when he wanted something to happen, really and truly, that it happened.  That thought alone raised a giddiness in him that far surpassed even when he first saw Light.

Because Turtle was everywhere.  He thought he was everywhere anyhow.  He was in the Light when it came, and in the Dark when it came, and he was in the Hard and the Soft as well.  He wasn’t sure that there was anything else except where he was.  It confused him a little bit because like when he couldn’t see anything, he knew it didn’t mean that there was only Nothing.  Like now, when the Dark came, he could no longer ‘see’ the Hard or the Soft, but he knew they were there.  He could almost ‘feel’ them.  But since he was in them as well as around them, he simply knew they were there without seeing them.

Turtle began, again, to get tired of the same thing over and over.  Again there was no variation.  Even though he enjoyed watching Light and Dark cover the Soft and Hard for a time… it became routine.  It became the same over and over.  Everything was so orderly.  He decided to ‘think’ things differently again.  So, he clumped all the hard and soft together in one place right in front of where he floated.
[Posted 1/14/2004 at 8:9 AM]

=== Tuesday January 13, 2004 ===

Turtle (Part 1)

Turtle sat in a very dark place, thinking.  Turtle thought far too often, about far too many things, and just now he began thinking about how he could not truly say if he was sitting, standing, or floating.  The reason for this is that Turtle existed in a dark place.  A place devoid of anything except himself really.  He decided that he should consider himself as floating as he couldn’t feel anything below him, above him, or before him.  He could not see anything either and, inevitably, began thinking about this more than anything else.

If I don’t see anything, does it exist? He thought to himself.  If I don’t see anything, or feel anything, does that not mean there is nothing else but me in this place? It was hard for him to even fathom what seeing might be like.  To be honest, he wasn’t sure if there wasn’t anything to see, or if he just couldn’t see what might be there.  Even this line of thinking began to confuse him, so he began simply to think about nothing once more.

Some time later.  And I say time because Turtle was fairly confident about time.  At least the passage of time.  He knew that some time ago he had been thinking about seeing, or hearing, or feeling something.  He just couldn’t say how long ago.  It was simply, in the past.  Of course, he only recently discovered the future.  Until that point he had only known the past and the present.  A moment just was, or it was in the past.  It wasn’t until he started saying to himself ‘I will think about seeing later, and in this moment I will think about nothing’ that he discovered the future.  Because, if something hadn’t happened yet, and he planned to do something but not just yet, it must not be in the past OR the present.

Needless to say, he was very excited about time.  It was a fairly easy thing for him to grasp.  Something was in the past, something was in the now, or something would be in the future.  But this ‘existence’ issue was bothering him.  He knew that he existed because he knew that he was thinking about things.  But he couldn’t tell if there was anything else there.  Just blackness, and silence, and nothing to touch.  He would have felt alone, but he had never existed in any other way than he did now.  So, he didn’t feel alone at all.

He just was.

Except, just being wasn’t enough.  Turtle began to think about the nothingness that surrounded him and he became unhappy.  At least, unhappy is what he considered himself, and as he was the only thing around, he must have been right.  He knew that when he was not unhappy, he thought a whole lot more about things and also made more plans.  And when he was unhappy, as he was now, he thought more and more about things he wasn’t sure about.

Now before we continue, you have to understand that Turtle didn’t even know it’s own shape.  In fact, it couldn’t prove that it was anything more than thought as it couldn’t feel anything at all around itself, and could not touch itself, it just wasn’t sure.  In the past, all the times before that Turtle had begun thinking and reached a particularly difficult thought, he would just stop thinking.  This time, Turtle was determined to keep thinking when things started confusing him.  When he next began to confuse himself, he would force himself to keep thinking.  No matter what.

It just so happened, that soon after this thought and plan of action crossed his mind, it came to pass that he was thinking of seeing.  This time, when he began to be confused about things not existing if they weren’t seen, he kept thinking.  If I can’t see something, it doesn’t mean that it doesn’t exist.  I can’t see myself, but I know that I exist. And, it’s about this time that he would have smiled had he known what that was, or had a body from which to grow a smile.  So, it’s possible that I’m not alone.  That there are things out there even if I can’t see or feel them.  Because I cannot see or feel myself, and I know I exist.

The funny thing is, right about this time, something changed.  Everything changed.  There was ‘something’ where once there was nothing.  It was almost as if he could see, except there was still nothing to see.  What now existed around him was the nothing that he had previously been ‘floating’ in, but now that nothing was mixed with the very new, and very exciting ‘something’.  Compared to the unhappy he had been feeling, Turtle was now very ecstatic.  Again, he would have smiled, except he still didn’t have anything to smile with.

He knew he existed because he could think.  And he knew he existed because he perceived both something and nothing swirling around him now constantly.  And he knew there was a then, a now, and a will be, because he now planned to think about the something in the very near future.  Except, he kept thinking, because he was close to being confused.  He didn’t want to keep calling what he saw around him something and nothing.  He decided, instead, to call the nothing Dark, and the something, Light.  Dark and Light.  I am not alone.

++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++

Shane

[Posted 1/13/2004 at 7:44 AM]

=== Sunday January 11, 2004 ===

Ashes, ashes...

We all fall down from time to time.  It's a part of the process.  And it's the process that I've always been so concerned about in my life.  I fear falling down.  It's not like a computer game, where I can restart from a save point.  Life is riskier, but life is also more rewarding.  And it isn't about how many times we fall down and scrape our knees, it's about how many times we get back up afterward.  It's about pushing forward, through everything that gets thrown our way.  It's how we can make it to the finish line and know that we've done it.  That life is exactly how it was supposed to be.  Pain, and happiness inclusive.

Happy Trails,

Shane

=== Saturday January 10, 2004 ===

Do you ever, do you never, do you sometimes...

He felt it slip, and suddenly, the weight of it hit him.  And that lightness of being left him like the last rays of sun through the trees before becoming silhouettes against a darkened sky.  He thought perhaps that Atlas felt this way, the sky his burden, and those rays his reward.  But that lightness, those rays, that being left him and he wanted it back desperately.  But it was like those dreams when he was  younger.  On the edge of reality, where existence ended, and the intanible clouds began.  All the fear in the world couldn't keep him away forever.  This fall was his own.

+++++++

locked in soulful indifference
a passionate vaccuum
embraced and let go

+++++++

=== Friday February 27, 2004 ===

Swimming like a fish...

I've begun swimming roughly every second day.  I love swimming every second day.  A day to recover the muscles and lungs only to dive in again the next day after that.  I swam competitively a long time ago, and love the water.  I'm feeling the old muscles getting back into shape.  Being able to stay under the water longer.  My ears are clearer than they have been in a while.  And you know what's one of my favourite things?  Just floating either face down in the water, or floating on my back in the water.  So my ears are blocked.  When everything goes quiet, but it's not really quiet.  You can hear your heart beating.  You can hear things clacking other things under the water.  But even though the noise is there, there's a stillness to it.  It's so peaceful.

Apparently even when I was too young to remember, I loved the water.  I don't doubt it.  Only because as long as I can remember, I've loved the water.  But more than any body of water, the ocean calls to me.  Even with Lake Ontario right at my doorstep, I feel so landlocked.  Lakes are beautiful, but the always feel less alive than the ocean.  Or, less... something.

Anyway, for now I'm going to say ciao.  May water welcome you with open waves.

Peace,

Shane

=== Wednesday February 25, 2004 ===

There isn't time for all but all we need.

For all we need, there is time. The trick of it is, to find what the need is. But I've been thinking, prompted by a question. The meaning of life? To me, it's almost too simple. The answer? The answer is the search for the meaning! It's the search that gives the meaning. I think that finding the answer would be our undoing. Well, for me it would be.

It's like how I used to think the afterlife would be like. Heaven. You'd suddenly know all the answers to what you had been looking for. You'd know everything. The thing of it is, that has always scared me. I dont' want to know all the answers just like that. It's the finding out that gives my life meaning. The learning. The experience.

It's the journey, not the destination. And I very honestly believe that death is far from the end of the journey. It's just another lesson learned along the way. Will I miss physical life when it's gone? I can say that I would... but I"m saying that from this point of view. Not the then point of view.

It's all so topsy turvy in my head. So yeah, I do think too often about some things. This latest thought was prompted, however, by a question from a friend. What's the meaning of life. I had to think about it. Didn't I? Can't let a challenge go unanswered.

For now I sleep. And I'm going to enjoy it.

As per usual. :-)

Shane
[Posted 2/25/2004 at 12:20 AM]

=== Monday February 23, 2004 ===

An Early Morning

I remember the sound the wind made through the trees.  I remember them speaking to me, of mischif, of love, of respect.  I remember the sweet smell of late Summer and Autumn.  Moon mountain, and it's rocky, barren face.  A testament to 'progress' but a land of endless possibility for a 7 year old.  Bedrock breaching the soil in endless supply.  Our last stand against the inferno, as we dug deep a mile away, taking what we needed, dumping what we didn't.  Creating mountains of black glass, and smoke, and ruin.

But, the grasses grew back, and the trees, and the bedrock once so prominent fading slightly.  Giving way to a different kind of progress.  Mother nature taking back what never belonged exclusively to us.  Not for that.  Not for destruction or greed.  Or need without reason.  Times have changed, for even me.  Who never walked 10 miles in the snow, uphil both ways.  Who never had to struggle from the earth to find food.  To find shelter.  To find love.

Times have changed, even for me.  Who never had to fear a man or woman would snatch me from the playground.  And the world spins with rage.  And we ride it out, some mad carnival ride going 10 speeds too fast.  Hanging on with horror, some with glee, some with their eyes closed and some with their eyes far too open for their own good.  But what I fear the most, is that if the world keeps spinning as fast as it is, if we don't try and change speeds... downshift, that we'll all be flung from it's back.  A distant memory.

A faded dream.

Peace,

Shane

Wow, okay, that's a bit bleak for a Monday morning, but it's a theme that comes back to me often.  I just wrote without direction above.  It started as a tribute to a little town I loved when I was younger.  Where my parents grew up, and my Grandparents set down roots.  And the smell of the tree that used to be behind her house.  A house she built with her husband from the ground up.  No basement, but a foundation of love.  Dedication.  And necessity.  It's funny how that could lead to the thoughts that followed.  Have a great Monday all!

[Posted 2/23/2004 at 8:34 AM]

=== Sunday February 22, 2004 ===

There is no wall, the sky is all...

Cat Stevens, Tori Amos, and Vienna Teng playing on speakers right now.  Mellow and quiet for tonight.  They'll take me away to both the future and to the past.  Watching the ocean on the left as I rode down Beach Road in Australia with my family, listening to 'Father and Son' or 'Tea for the Tillerman".  No better place than in those long-grass days of youth and summer.  Well, there are better places, but some days, there are no better places than those of our past.  Savouring life the way it was.  Loving every tear and smile dug out from the past.  Releshing the emotion of your life gone by.  And yet to come.

I think I'm going to rest my eyes now, and my body and soul.  Work starts again tomorrow, but there are no walls around me.  I'm still in my summer, and the sky doesn't even pretend to be a limit.  Sometimes life overwealms me, but in a good way.  There's so damn much out there it scares me witless sometimes.  It freezes my progress and stills my tongue.  Everything I expected my 23'rd year to be, everything I hope my 24'th to be.  It isn't as I'd thought.  It never is.  This life, the last life, and the one beyond the veil.  I'm sure I've been on the cusp before.  Teetering in a dream, between solid reality and the whispy truth of clouds and fuzzy dreams.  Elation is a potion.

I'm so thirsty.

But more than that, I'm tired.  I know I'm understood far more than I sometimes think when I write like this.  Scattered words, these words.  I'm not the only one.  My credo.  I'm not the only one to be like this.  To think like this.  To need what I need, or desire what I desire.

Sweet Dreams and Goodnight,

Shane

[Posted 2/22/2004 at 10:29 PM]

=== Saturday February 21, 2004 ===

Saturday is my Sabbath

I don't  know why this came to mind to me, but I noticed something about my patterns.  Saturday, later at night, is my time of reflection.  Even when I'm out and about on a Saturday, I'm introspective.  Saturdays are my days of thought, reflection, thanks, and forward thinking.  My time of prayer, creation, and sometimes my time of melancholy.

I had a dream come back to me from last night sometime during the day today.  I just suddenly remembered.  It was night in the dream, and I was in a modern village of some sort nestled in the woods.  I remember walking.  I remember other people.  I remember a cargo elevator.  I also remember mountains/hills around.  It was pitch dark night, but that area felt like home.  It's strange, but my memories are few of the dream last night.  I just remember knowing where I was, and where I was going.  Last night wasn't about being chased either.  It was just me, and this place, and the people that were around.  Refreshingly different.

I think I'm going to rest my eyes now.  I'm tired tonight.

Shane

[Posted 2/21/2004 at 10:57 PM]

=== Wednesday February 18, 2004 ===

It's a need like any other...

Another surreal moment today.  No particular reason.  Just that sense of being 'between' everything and not a part of it at the same time.  I also feel a calling.  A need for travel.  I used to like to think that I had some gypsy in me.  And, I suppose that's possible, if you go back far enough.  My Great Grandfather was adopted in Italy and never, ever talked about where he came from before that moment in time.  So, I like to think... but that might be the writer in me.  And maybe, just perhaps, having that writer in me is just like having a calling to travel.  It's a need like any other.  I need to experience new things.  New places.  New people.  I was reflecting on all the people, good people, I've let slip from my life.  It comes from the difficulty for me to maintain as many close friendships as I sometimes foster.  In friendships, I like to be close.  It's just how I am.  It's my personality type, it's my... it's me.

Once and a while I'll grab on to a friend, and that closeness will come naturally, and sometimes it lasts a long time.  Sometimes, drifting apart is a natural event.  It still doesn't stop me from mourning a friendship fading.  And still, I know that they come back just the same.  Friends drift in and out of your life.  There's so many people out there.  And I want to know all of them.  Everyone deserves to be known.  It's just what I believe.  We all come from somewhere, and we all have stories behind who we are.  And I find it constantly fascinating.

Anyway, I'm so very tired.  I'm going to bed early tonight.  Maybe I'll get 8 hours sleep!

It would be good.

Peace,

Shane

[Posted 2/18/2004 at 9:38 PM]

=== Wednesday February 18, 2004 ===

You want words from me,
assurances, and affirmations
love, the forever kind.

You don't believe
that I could ever, scream
my devotion from the rooftops.

That I could make it real,
tangible, breathable.

That I could make it about you
that it is about you
that you are worth being about.

You don't believe me when I tell you
that the future is for you
that the now is for you

You don't believe me,
but I believe in you.

Shane

=== Sunday February 15, 2004 ===

I asked her to open her eyes, but she didn't want to look at me. I wasn't sure if it was the sun at my back, or the clouds in the distance, but she couldn't face me in that light. We had come this far together, hand in hand, but in this heat, our hands became slick, and we slipped. From each other, forces pulling us apart.

I think she left me long before I said goodbye. It reminded me of dancing between the rain. The way she slid away, slowly between my blinks. We tried to fly, but too close, to the sun or to each other. A tangle and a tumble, and the stormclouds in the distance.

I turned to her then, and told her that I liked storms. That the lightning made me feel more alive. That the thunder pulsed through my blood. That the wind gave me goosebumps. She didn't know how to court a watersign. And, I was a watersign through and through. True to my nature.

But I never betrayed her.

I betrayed her.

But I never betrayed her.

I lost her.

But I never betrayed her.

I betrayed us.

And I love her. And I love her. And I love her.

And I lost her.

But there are so many thens, and only one now. This is the only place I've ever been. The right now. The exactly this moment. The instant. This instant.

And I love her still.

She still makes me smile. But for memory. And she still makes me laugh, but for her ghost. And she still believes in me somehow, and hates me, and loves me all the same. But she doesn't understand, or rather, I don't understand still. There's so much to this. All the mistakes and the non-mistakes I've made. Brought me here. Brought me now.

And I love her.

And I always will.
[Posted 2/15/2004 at 10:22 PM]

=== Sunday February 15, 2004 ===

Those I have Loved

I've been in love a few times in my life. And, for the mostpart, even though I may not be in love with those same people any more... it's safe to say I love them still. Each one has a hold on a part of my heart and each one has meant something in my life. Each one has seen me change just a little bit in my growing towards who I'm meant to become. Love is an important thing to me, hell, it's an important thing to anyone I think. It's how each of us define love that often differs.

I suppose I might be more depressed right now than I am if I kept brooding about currently being alone. The truth of it is, I am alone right now because I've chosen to be alone, and I'm not doing anything active right now to find someone special for my life. I've found myself slipping into the persona of the 'brooding writer' in social situations. Not emphasizing the 'writer' part simply because I don't always have a pad and pen in my hand, but the brooding comes to the fore rather quickly at times. I don't know how I feel about that. I never used to be this kind of brooding, but I'm starting to revel in the fact that I am me.

I'm in love with putting words to the page. I love when my muse breathes her voice into my mind and our words dance across the page. Our union for all to see. A pure mingling of passions, and kindling of life in an otherwise void space.

That being said, Happy Valentine's Day to all of you out there. I may not have my true love in my arms tonight, but I'll find her. A love to make true. And then we'll dance. And the stars will blink, as always, with jealousy... and the moon will light our way. Hopeless romantic? Maybe. But, life's too short not to make your dreams alive like this. She's out there, and I think I'm almost, finally, ready to start looking again. This journey is just beginning.

Peace, and sweet dreams,

Shane
[Posted 2/15/2004 at 12:57 AM]

=== Friday February 13, 2004 ===

"I've got a theory... it could be bunnies..."

For the last few days, things around me have seemed so surreal.  I can't put my finger on it, but everything from the news to just walking down the street has been a surreal event for me.  It just feels like change.  It doesn't frighten me, it doesn't excite me, it just is, and I swear, it seems so surreal.  Last night, as I fell asleep (or the night before) I went into a meditative state.  I figured, since my body was so tired, I would experiment with my awake mind.  I tried shifting my focus from place to place.  Foot, hand, arm, face.  I tried focusing on each part in turn.  In those moments, every other part faded away from my awareness.  It was an interesting feeling.  Sometime after that, I must have fallen asleep because my memories fades at that point.

It's just interesting to me that the whole world seems so surreal right now.  I feel like everything's wrong.  Just a gut feeling kind of thing.  Or, rather, not that everything's wrong, but that things are different than they should be.  It's like remembering something that hasn't happened yet.  At least, if I were to describe the sensation, that's how I would describe it.  Now, what I'm not sure about is why I have this feeling.  Is it because I'm starting to realize that there's so much horror in the world?  Is it because I stand constantly on the cusp of one change or another?  Is it the way the sky has been the past few days?  The mild weather?  My desire for things I wish I had, or wish I didn't have?  There's just so many different factors it's hard to narrow down where this stems from.

Just more introspection.  I'm one for introspection if nothing else.

So, things are feeling surreal, but not necessarily bad, or wrong.  Just different.  Sigh.  Sometimes words do fail me.  It's not how many words you know, but what you can do with the ones you have.  Right now, this is all I can do.  We'll see what the weekend brings.  Hope all of you out there have a good weekend, and enjoy the days and enjoy the nights.  Each cycle is precious.

Peace,

Shane

[Posted 2/13/2004 at 5:35 PM]

=== 4 Comments ===

Aloha,

Well that was a meditative post.  Heh, you're updating faster than I can comment!

Laying down Meditation
I had to do that for a Transpersonal Psychology course.  One guy fell asleep and snored for 30 mins because he said it was so relaxing.  Well he was a Football player so no one would say anything to him.  Heh.  We had to 'feel' our toes with our mind, then move across the whole body from foot to head.  That was interesting, and I sometimes do that, but I make sure I'm on the cold floor because it keeps me awake.  Heh, supposedly lying on the floor once a day is supposed to be restful or enlightening.

Improvement
Ooh, por favor, but I noticed the word 'change'.  That gives me chills.  I have long philosophies about how that word affects things.  Which is why I like saying improvement, since I see change as like changing form, but improvement as evolving.  Once a friend said, "What, are you a Revolutionary?"  I replied, "No...  I'm an...  Evolutionary."  He was like, "Whoa."  Heh.  Yeah, I like to live, to exist, and to create for the sake of evolution for myself and for society.  That is my one driving goal, which I have to think about because it is surely too hard to do alone--but I want to evolve this society so that kids like my friend won't be afraid to tell his parents he is gay, for fear of being beaten up; in a world where humans are truly judged by their own skills, but also knowing that each person has their special ability and place...  Oh so much.  *Sigh*  Thinking about that brings me down, because I remember my oldest and best friend telling me, "That's nice dreams."  And I was like, "No, it is a hope.  And before I die, I want to make sure as many people as possible have that 'hope' as well, because if it exists in their minds, it has the potential to become true and to spread...  And one day, long after I've died, there will be a truly free world."

Ooh, I have to stay away from these thoughts.  8)  I'm supposed to be healing from last week's heart problems.  Vincent is not yet ready to be the full Rising Sun.  But soon, I will.  8)

Be good, see light all around you, and good things will come to you...  Do bad...  And...

Smile!

Vince

=== Friday February 13, 2004 ===

you were my ally in the older days
before the trees gave way to glass
and hungry hearts called from the spires

you were my friend within the older days
to watch the willows by the river
translate from the earth to sky

you were my love among the older days
the focus of my true devotion
ever present in my beating heart

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++

time moved slowly as that river,
spires grew instead of trees
it never fails to make me shiver
that we'd give up such things as these

autmn breezes through the branches
waters pure and crips and clean
or the darkest sky and bright stars
but for the light cannot be seen.

+++++++++++++++++++++++++++

And I awoke from river's edge.  Covered in the peace that had fulfilled me in that place.  I hit snooze time and again, almost at the extent of being late for work this morning.  I didn't want to leave that place of trees and water and sky.  It reminded me of something I feel I've lost in myself.  That forest I used to embrace within me, and that ocean that I long for late at night.  The wild world, at peace with itself, in balance.  I know I've been there before.  I can almost remember how the air tastes.  I can almost feel the light.  It used to be so real, and everywhere I go it seems to slowly fade.  Further and further from my mind, and yet, from time to time I see it in a tree by a river.  The wholeness of it all.  How it still connects me back to that place where things are purer.  A sillhouette, the sound of a river, the dark sky above with roiling clouds flowing by.

And that is what I long for.  Those trees, and that water.  The air that lifts me up, and the sky that keeps me awed in wonder.

And I've been there before.  And, I pray, I make it back there again.

Peace,

Shane

=== Wednesday February 11, 2004 ===

I thought for a while
as if you were there
and I smiled
turning to share an insight

to the air...

+++++++++++++++++

Sometimes I just want to keep going, typing these words down on this decreasingly blank space.  Just let it all flow out of me.  Sometimes I feel that even if I wrote day in and day out, all that I wanted to write to the page would not be written in full, and that slows my ascent.  I think, when I cannot write, it is not my muse who abandons me but rather my courage that abandons me.  And I, in turn, abandon she, my muse.  I've got so many stories to tell, so many beginnings and so many ends.  All of it I want to get on to the page, but things keep getting in the way.  Life, sure, but that wasn't always the case.  Even when I didn't work in the same way as I do now.  Even when I was absolutely without stress, everything flowed so much more smoothly.

I sometimes picture myself an old man, frantically writing thoughts to the page for fear of my time runing out.  And what really gets me is that I don't know when my time will run out.  And I have so much more to say.  And I want to have a child, and a wife.  I want to teach my children about life, about the world, about my beliefs, and other people's beliefs as well.  I want to teach them that it's okay to choose, and it's okay to think, and that it's okay to love, even for a fear of loss.  Of course, when I think about that, I think that it would be my children reteaching me their own brand of unconditional love that gets changed along the way.  Again, by life and circumstance.

I know there will be a great many people who would disagree with my belief that we are all inherently good.  At least, we all start that way.  Well, I believe we all start tabula rasa.  I know that my own beliefs may be slanted, because I always strive to see the good in people.  I fight always in my mind for the person who is on the short end of the stick.  Many times, it's people who may be thought of as broken that are in that position.

God, I don't know.  Just thinking.  Lunch is over now.

Be well,

Shane

[Posted 2/11/2004 at 2:59 PM]

=== Wednesday February 11, 2004 ===

Kinda-sorta middle of the road

Well it's Wednesday again, my ear popped a little bit this morning offering slightly better treble hearing than yesterday as well as releiving some pressure from within my head.  There's currently no pain at all, so I think I'm going to ride this out as it seems to only be getting better.  I will, however, wear ear-plugs of some sort next time I swim.  It's the least I can do to my ear for being so decent to me despite my neglect.  I still should get my ears checked though.  Even before this incident I'd noticed a growing 'What?' factor every time I had a conversation with someone.  A large decline in hearing definately runs in the family, but I'm hoping that at 24, it's just a matter of getting rid of anything that might be blocking the passage of sound.

I did dream last night.  Scattered dreams, much fading now, but dreams that I remember hitting snooze one more time to get back into.  A familiar scenario.  The setting being a shopping mall complex of some sort.  There were people from my Grade school present.  And that was a long time ago.  I'm also just about through 'Golden Fool' by Robin Hobb.  This series The Tawny Man series, is definatly a page turner.  Of course, you'd have to read The Farseer trilogy to fully appreciate the trio.  It's an interesting world that Robin creates.  Just enough politics, a certain type of magic, and characterization to make the world come to life.

If I had a penny every time I wrote here that I've once again been neglecting reading all your sites I'd be a rich... well, I'd have closer to a dollar than nothing.  It's not for lack of wanting, but more for lack of time to fit all my wantings in to one day.  Caught up in a few things lately.  The books being one of them.  I go through binges of reading.  Mostly when I chance upon an author that continually draws me in.  Charles De Lint is one such auther.  Robin Hobb is another.  I will come around, if not as often then with as much voracity to read what's been going on in all of your lives.

Till then, Have a good one!

Shane

[Posted 2/11/2004 at 8:21 AM]

=== Sunday February 8, 2004 ===

Mirrors and Truth and the difference between...

Something I remember from Highschool English class is the idea of a theme in writing. Some kept coming back over and over. "Appearances can be deceiving" is one that struck me the hardest. It's a theme that continues to echo in life each day. Things aren't always as they seem. People say one thing, mean another, and do yet another. In fact, we often even deceive ourselves. I'd like to say I learned much from this theme. It's reoccurence again and again in my life, and that I always look past the surface. That I always see things a little more closer to the truth than they sometimes appear.

The truth of the matter is, however, that it is not always that way. Sometimes perhaps, but not nearly enough, can I actually say I'm seeing. Our eyes take in our surroundings and sometimes things slip through the cracks of observation. The fact is, somewhere, there is a reason for all we see. And a reason behind the reason. The man with the sour look on the corner, walking quickly without looking side to side. He just found out that someone he cared greatly about died. And he's angry because he never got to tell her what he wanted to. He's angry at himself, and he can't see past that anger. He isn't a bad person, but in that instance, looking at him from your own side of the street... you may see someone you wouldn't want to know.

It's something I have to keep teaching to myself every day. That everyone is coming from somewhere. Everyone has reasons for the things they do.

Just thought I'd write about that. And in other news, I'm currently mostly deaf in my left ear. It's got a constant dull ache since I went swimming and it didn't unclog like I had hoped. Needless to say, swimming was a good experience because I haven't been in the water like that in too long. One of my favourite things to do is hold my breath under water. I'll just lie forward and float, drifting away. Hearing only my heartbeat tha-thump tha-thump. Getting slower as I try to conserve the oxygen I do have in me. Not thinking, but just being. It's so peaceful. I love the water... and miss the ocean more than I could say in writing.

I'm heading to bed now, hoping that my ear will unclog without problems. It'd be nice to wake up to a full circle of audio perception. But, beggars can't be choosers, and hopefully my dreams will offer me clearer senses.

Sweet dreams,

Shane
[Posted 2/8/2004 at 9:0 PM]

=== Wednesday February 4, 2004 ===

Morning Vigil

It's 8:20 and I have 10 minutes before I begin work.  I could dive in to work early, but I usually stay later anyhow, and these 10-20 minutes every morning is what allows me to 'wind up' to work.  Put my headphones on, and I'm not actually here at work.  I'm just writing, and listening to music.  I fade into the shadows.

I have an 'origami a day' calendar. I spend a few minutes creating something that should be a work of art, and only falls short a little bit by being 'folded paper not quite appearing to be art'.  But that's on account of my troubles with trying to fold symmetrically.  These troubles boggle my mind, on account of my childhood obession with symmetry.  Leggo.  All of my leggo creations had to be symmetrical or they seemed wrong somehow.

I'd love to hear anyone with such childhood obessions... as it would ease my mind about my own.  However, as I've grown, I've found myself enjoying even more the creation of things that are slightly not symmetrical.  Dischord creating harmony... or something like that.

You'll have to bear with my ramblings in the morning, especially this morning.  No dreams remembered, nothing of note to talk about except my morning routine.  At least, for today.  I haven't been able to go around to any other sites as often in the recent past due to my computer being overhauled.  Well, I'm overhauling it by choice.  I dove in to a world that I don't think I'm ready for, but I'm determined to see it through.

Mandrake Linux.  Some of you may be familiar with this operating system.  I've found, much to my pleasant surprise, that I can get certain programs that will allow certain other 'windows' programs to run within Mandrake Linux.  Without the needless instability or constant problems through viruses or 'adware' programs.

All I really need is a computer that can play music, has an editor, and from time to time, a game I can lose myself in when I choose.  And now?  To work. To get lost in reality for a while.

Ciao for now,

Shane

[Posted 2/4/2004 at 8:51 AM]

=== Tuesday February 3, 2004 ===

The Dreamtime in the meantime -- Or how the sky keeps falling

Other than just the regular dreams I have, there's a different kind of state I get into when doing the 'cat-nap' thing.  I used to cat-nap during lunch at work, and still take naps on the bus or train coming out of the city after work.  (Or in to the city for that matter.)  Needless to say, I do experience something like dreaming in this state.  Except, I never remember what they consisted of.  It feels like I go inside myself.  I mean, that's the best example I have to describe what happens.  It almost feels like I close my eyes, and reach a place between sleep and awake.  Like my sub-concious is revisiting old memories, old places, creating a show for itself... but I never remember except for glimpses of colour.

More to come... work starts now, so I should cut this short.

[Posted 2/3/2004 at 8:31 AM]

=== Monday February 2, 2004 ===

God, I just woke up from my first nightmare in, oh, I don't know... about 4 years now.  Not the, 'oh my gosh, something's chasing me' kind of dream.  As I said, those are adventures.  This type of dream is a reoccuring nightmare of sorts.  I say of sorts because something's always different, but the situation is always similar.

I'm lying in my bed as it is now, in my room as it is now, and I think I'm awake.  I feel at least half-awake, and someone else is in my room.  It starts coming towards the bed.  I struggle to wake up, but it's hard.   Invariably, I wake up only to slip back to sleep almost right away, as if a hand is trying to pull me back to sleep.  I usually start trying to vocalize at this point, in my dream, probably out loud too.  What just happened though... the thing that walked in to my room in my just now waking dream.  The person I should say... at first it looked like someone I know.  My uncle Ron, except younger.  Then it started to walk into my room, and I realized it was wearing large glasses, they seemed oversized.  I noticed something else at that point... it seemed to be a she.

I started vocalizing before it started walking in the room.  I remember saying "who are you?" and then, three times I whisper-screamed, "uncle ron, uncle ron, uncle ron" because it's so hard to talk when I'm in that waking-sleep.  Around the third time, I was pulling out of the dream.

I'm writing this now as opposed to sleeping because it's the kind of lingering feeling, and lingering dream that I know is waiting for me just on the other side of conciousness.  I had forgotten how that kind of terror feels like.  See, in this dream that just passed.  I remember feeling that it was a dream, and I wanted to run it through because I know that it can't hurt.  That's why I asked it's name.  I've never done that in the past.  But there was no reply, just the moving towards me.

It seemed tall too.  It's head was coming to just under the top of my door frame... I think.  That part's fuzzy.  The strange part is, there was no transition to that dream and the fun one I was just having right before that one.  Well, the less scary, more interesting one.  I was in a building complex, work and live kind of complex.  I was in the garage part, and I got something out of the car that was there.  A two door.  Then I was going to head up to work.  Then, all of a sudden, must have been around 2:30, in real life, I go from this car-dream and I'm in my bed.  A waking dream, because my room is as it is now, except, enter strange presence.

Freaky, and damn.  I thought those nightmares were over.

Well, I think I'm okay now.  I"m going to try to enter in to some kinf of semblance of sleep for at least a couple of hours.  Hope you all are sleeping more soundly than I.

Sweet dreams,

Shane

[Posted 2/2/2004 at 2:37 AM]

=== Wednesday March 31, 2004 ===

I've known perfection...

I remember a post-rainy day when I was 5 years old.  Streets just saturated with water.  The kind of day I absolutely love.  Slightly overcast, trees all sillhouetts against a brilliantly grey sky.  The bright kind of grey that hides a rainbow, to show it briefly once and a while.  I remember the streets being empty.  They became my playground.  I owned the street that day.  The day and time felt magical to me.  And not just in the way that looking back over some childhood memories is magical.  I remember the feeling of electricity in the air.  I had a stick.  I saw a drain.  I plunged the stick into the sewer grate and expected it to be lost.  Up it popped, out of the grate, and onto the street again.  This grate was overflowing with water.  I kept pushing the stick back through the slots of the grate (it was a larger stick, not just a twig) and it kept shooting back up from the grate.  I was absolutely mystified.  It was as if an unseen hand kept pushing the stick back to me.  Then, on my last attempt, it did not return to me.

Now, that's pretty much all I remember from that day, save my running back to tell my parents about the magic.  And that, my friends, is a little piece of perfection from my past.  How much awe the world gave me.  And an indication of how I sometimes feel when walking through a forest, or feeling the summer rain on my face.  There's so much out there.  So much magic in the world just waiting to be appreciated.  Sure, we've learned that some things float, and some things sink.  But think about it without thinking about the science behind it... or even with thinking about the science behind it.

So, enjoy  those moments of perfection when they come to you.  Those moments when it clicks and you feel it.  It.  That overpowering sense of rightness.  Even amidst the bad days it's there.  The fact that you and I exist.  Are here now.  Me writing, and you reading, is mystifying.  All the sequences of events that brought us to this point.  Every time I moved from one house to another.  Every time I was sick.  Every time I went swimming.  Ever time I felt joy or pain.  Without absolutely everything happening to me exactly the way it did, I wouldn't be here in the way I am now.  I'd be different.  I may sometimes think about the past, and even think about regret... but I can't regret the past.  It's beyond change.  And it made me who I am.  Not perfect, but exactly who I'm meant to be right now, right here, at this time in my life.

And it counts for all of you too.  That you're here, that I read about your lives, and vice - versa.  Lets just say, I appreciate all that brought me to this point, and appreciate that you are all here as well.

The world, it most definately, an interesting place in which to live.

Peace,

Shane

[Posted 3/31/2004 at 3:49 PM]

=== Tuesday March 30, 2004 ===

All things in time, and all things for a reason.

The Sun keeps rising,
So too the Moon, after Sun
Chasing always, dawn.

Rise from your ashes
Embrace the flight you now seek,
follow now, the Moon.

Moon keeps you moving,
lighting the path to escape
Seek the beginning.

+++

Shane

=== Monday March 29, 2004 ===

Till I'm there; wish you were here...

I spent some time thinking about
all the things we never did,

and all the things we never talked about.

I hate that the opportunity to know you more
has been taken away from me.

I regret that I didn't take that opportunity
when I had it in my grasp.

You weigh heavy on my mind
not just as a lost friend,
but as all my lost opportunities
all my faded moments with loved ones
and all things I have not done.

You are that voice, the echo to my own,
it's raging pantomime and ragged sentiment
trying to discover life beyond life
and sound beyond the music of your memory.

And bittersweet, I loved them, every one
each jagged thorn and growing flower.

And peace,

And peace has come for you

but mine will have to wait.

+++

Shane

[Posted 3/29/2004 at 1:38 AM]

=== Thursday March 25, 2004 ===

Make mine a double

Nothing much to report or talk about.  It's
Wednesday.  Well, technically, it's Thursday now.  So...
happy Thursday.  And thanks to all of you for your comments.
I love getting feedback on my poetry.  It's part of my
escape.  The other part is not yet here.  Sometimes I think
I'd just like to pick up and start to travel.  Working odd jobs
and living.  Just being.  Different places.  Different
people.  Lots of stories.

Sometimes I think I would have done well in the 60's.

But would I have made it to 2000?

So make mine a double.  Of whatever you're having.  If
it's sleep, thank God, because I feel as though I need a double of that.

Peace,

Shane

=== Wednesday March 24, 2004 ===

Echoes in Empty Spaces
by Shane Fera

You read these syllables aloud inside your head,
knowing all of them ammount to just a single thought
just one constant devotion
an 'I want you' voiced in the silence that comes
from knowing that you're there

I fear it.  It.  That word that follows me around.
That question.
Are you happy?  Are you content?

I'm happy when I see the world smile.
I cry with Jupiter
I mourn with the Sun.

And you keep reading these words
wondering if they mean more than

this. following. that.

I can say I'll never be content
because there's so much out there to do, to be.

I say I will find happiness, beyond contentment.

I say too much and feel just this one, small, thing.

That I love you.

You help me feel.

You.

[Posted 3/24/2004 at 1:2 AM]

=== Sunday March 21, 2004 ===

More's the Pity

It would be nice.  Extremely and wonderfully nice,  if I could draw on inspiration in the instants that I desired it's aid.  Today I saw a couple of movies... both of which inspired me.  In fact, movies often inspire me.  Even the crappy movies.  I think it's more the environment that gets me going.  I start to really 'feel' it, you know?  A dark theatre, people huddled into rows, all watching the same thing.  There's an energy there that I can't get enough of.  Needless to say, I always get struck with the best ideas right in the middle of movies at theatres.  I get the ideas and then tell myself I can't wait to get home so I can write.  Well.. I'm here, and I can't find the inspiration any more.  I'm not in a darkened theatre, and I'm not watching a movie.  I'm just here, writing these words, trying to feel even a little of the inspiration that I felt this afternoon in the theatre.

Maybe it takes some training?  Or some dark and brooding music.  Or a glass of wine, or the conversation of friends.  Or perhaps it takes complacency, or solitude.  For me, it seems to take me being otherwise occupied.  If I'm currently not able to write down my thoughts, lord knows I'll probably get inspired.

Location, location, location.

Needless to say (an expression I have to find a few synonyms for) I so desperately want to write, and it's a hunger that only keeps growing.

But mostly, I want to write to Her.  And to be quite honest, right now I don't even know where She is, or who really...  all things in time.  But... it's about time.  I think I'm just about ready.

Cheers,

Shane

[Posted 3/21/2004 at 11:46 PM]

---

=== Sunday March 21, 2004 ===

Lost to the Noise, Drowning in Music

It's the music that moves me, not you that keeps me.  It's the turning that spins me to life.  Dark and brooding, sensuality, I lose myself in their voices, in their notes.  I am a note.  I become a word, a sound, and I'm lost again.  Drifting in and out, crescendo, decrescendo.

I am a sound, in a prayer, in a song, in the voice of someone singing me to life at night... long after the stars flicker to life and the moon carpets the ground.

++++++++++++

Let me say this.  I often think.  Or, rather, I think often?  *shrug*  I suppose both are just as acceptable.  What I mean to say.  How I mean to feel is this:  Have you ever pictured a scene in your head.  Inspired from something.  Anything.  A song, a movie, a smell.  Have you ever suddenly saw a scene of something in your head in which you knew you were a part of even if it wasn't really the you that you are?

Confused yet?

For me, my mind often creates things, scenes in my head.  Parts of a story yet untold.  Characters that I bring to life in my mind.  That I know much more than I can conciously relate.  It's to these snippets that I often feel I belong.  It's to these characters I've become a part of.  I almost feel their emotion.  Hell, I do feel their emotion.  It's just like losing yourself for just a moment.  And I wonder at those times, when I have to shake my head a little to get myself out of the daydream.  I wonder what might happen if I do lose myself in part of a story yet untold.

Just another thought I guess, passing through my head early Sunday morning.

+++++++++++++++++++++

For now, sweet dreams all of you.Peace,Shane

[Posted 3/21/2004 at 2:2 AM]

=== Monday March 15, 2004 ===

As silent, in courtship
By Shane Fera

I think I'll call you perfection,
Something granted after a long night's slumber
And a deep and heady dream

I think I'll call you Philomel
You sang me to sleep more times than I remember
I embrace your memory

I think I'll call you Justice or Peace
Having shown in my life both the truth and falacy
You betray yourself

You are so many things, so many names,
A contradiction seeking sustenance; drinking me,
and Fueling chaos.

But passion, passion, passion, you are worth that pain.

03/15/2004

Posted on 03/14/2004
Copyright © 2004 Shane Fera

=== Friday March 12, 2004 ===

Somehow, I don't think so...

This week has been a good week for my confidence at work.  I'm confident, I'm getting through the 'trouble tickets', and I'm getting a raise to get me to the level of everyone else at work.  My situation is a little different than most where I work.  I started off as 'call handler' which is really 'glorified secretary' when it comes down to it.  And, I loved the job.  It was without much stress, I could talk with the clients, and I learned about the software and hardware we had out there.  It was a great entry level for the company.   So, I'm gettin' on gettin' on.

And like I always say, if the grass is green, why not stay and graze a while?

Well, I've never said that before, but maybe it can be something I always say in the future.

I'm trying to put money away to do many things.  Go back to school and pursue my interest in Psychology.  Buy a condo in Toronto.  Travel.  Did I mention Travel?  The good part of the condo is that I can rent it out when I decide (if?) to just pick up and travel for a year.  Or not.  It's all up in the air folks, but it's all up there somewhere.  It's all good, more importantly, and though I'm constantly knocking on wood, I think I'm in a decent place.

*knock on wood*

So, there you have it.  That's where I've been.  Just being.  And I think I'm going to enjoy the summer this year, more than last year.  I'm looking forward to biking.  I'm looking forward to Toronto in the summer.

I'm looking forward to Toronto in the Fall.

Hope you're all doing well in your own corners of the earth.  I still read, if not always comment.
Peace,Shane

=== Monday March 8, 2004 ===

Two paths diverged within a wood...

That poem, but Robert Frost, of two paths diverging in a wood.  I've often wondered if I would have chosen the well used path, or the less used path.  The path less travelled by.  I mostly fairly certain that I'd have taken the path less travelled.  Just now though, I think I knew with more than just a certainty that I'd choose no path at all.  I'd stand there looking down both paths and going over all I'd gain and lose with each.

two paths diverged within a wood
and I chose no path whatsoever

I choose life! Well, I choose to write the word life over and over again on the page.  I constantly choose this word or that and do not instead choose to move one foot in front of the other.  I'm working and living well, and meeting some new people, and getting by just fine.  I'm growing up, I'm branching out, I'm reaching up, I'm...

...desperately trying to cut my limbs from my body so I'll realize finally what I'm missing.  I'm desperately trying to prove to myself that I'm needing to go in another direction.  I write truth.  I write truth in my stories, and stories in my lies, and lies in my truths.  I grow wings and shed feathers just as fast.  I experience a moment of clarity, and take it in.  And keep on walking towards the bus stop or train station.  Waiting.  For something.  I'm waiting for something to happen, and I don't even know what the hell it is.

I'm just waiting.  Waiting for my time to come.  I hate waiting.  I despise just standing there at a bus stop.  I usually start walking in the direction of my destination hoping that I'll reach the next bus stop by the time it drives by.  I don't like not moving towards my destination.

i don't have a destination

I believe in purpose.  I believe I have one.  Should I just wait for it?  Or should I wag the dog?

God. I even try and make these moments when I'm so together I'm coming apart feel like a piece of art.  I'm an artist, and I've hardly had any training as an artist.  Or a writer.  I have no idea how to make money being an artist or a writer.  I know all too well that expression 'starving artist' and 'bohemia' are a large part of what I have to look forward to if I just dive in. I believe in art.  I believe in emotion.  I believe in the strong union of the two.  I'm an artist, and I'm working in tech support to make money.  I'm still writing and I'm still growing.  And I'm always feeling that I'm just here.  Here.  Trying to get 'There' without a compass, or a roadmap, or enough proactivity to raise an umbrella after it starts raining.  I've always lived in one world dreaming of another.

the grass is always greener...

...greener than money

He asked me 'brother can you spare a dime?'
and I said 'Yes sah! I surely can, here take a dollar'
Then I offered him a poem, and he told me that he couldn't eat a poem.

And here I've always thought I could live forever in a poem.  Words strung together in a 'nice' way.

But I've never 'needed' in my life.  I've never had to fight my way to the top of anything.  I've never had to struggle for a crumb.  So, naturally, poetry comes easy for me.

Naturally, I've always had time to wallow through my emotions and philosophise.

I feel like Atlantis before it decided to sink.  I feel like Troy.  I feel like Pompeii.

I am a gathering storm.

Time to rest a while,

Work tomorrow.

Peace.

Shane

[Posted 3/8/2004 at 2:0 AM]

=== Thursday March 4, 2004 ===

A shallow breath, and eerie depth...

I couldn't help myself.  I had to be here.  I had to see you one last time before it... all came undone.  But not like the song, messier than that, coming apart at the seams only means that love takes a different shape.  And shapes in the dark shift and grow in shadow.

But as I said, there could be no other course, no other path to our union.  The storm grew when we met, and broke when we parted.  And like all storms, I drank it all in with wild eyes, and a wild heart.  I'm tame, but I can't be tamed.  I'm a rock, but you can't build a house on my ground.  Don't expect my waters to glitter with hidden gold, nor sparkle with sunken diamonds.  I am as you see me here.  So simple in design.  And I love you.

I love you.

But I can't dance with your shadows, or fly with your reflection.  Not forever.  What starts in a dream has to end in a touch.  And as much as my hands reach, you sift through my fingers.

And I can't stay here.

Though I'd stay here forever.

I have to move on, I'm not meant to remain.

I need to touch you.  To look in your eyes and feel your soul.  I need your voice raised in argument, and your voice raised in song.  I need your breath mixed with mine, and I need to share your passion.  And I need you to share mine.

And I need.

But I couldn't help myself.  Not this one last time.  To dance next to your memory and mingle with your ghosts.

So I say this in parting,

Goodnight and goodbye my love,

Shane

[Posted 3/4/2004 at 12:15 AM]

=== Tuesday March 2, 2004 ===

What is tomorrow?

I just don't know anymore. Tomorrow is an illusion.

I find myself drifting more and more from one moment to the next. I've got a job which I do enjoy despite the stress at times. But, interestingly enough, the stress goes away when I start thinking about the realization that I don't 'need' it. There are always choices in life. Always paths to walk. For me, my productivity goes down when I get stressed. It's because of my personality type. So, I force myself to realize that I don't need it. That it could all fall away, and I'd still have my words. It could all fall away, and I'd still have my skills. It could all fall away and I'd have everything I am. Still. Just realizing that all I really need to get by is with me always makes me calm down. Less stress. More fun.

I'm a writer. I'm realizing that more and more also. I don't care how anyone else chooses to classify 'writer'. Yes, I've only published a poem here and there. But I'm a writer to my very core. My words are who I am. And who I yearn to be, and who I loath being. They are what I create with. Paint with. Express with. I'm a writer, and my words are all I'll ever need to get by.

Whatever else may come, so be it. I'm lovin' every minute of it. Every heartache, every joy, ever person in my life feeds the fire.

I love all of it.

Bring it on.

Shane
[Posted 3/2/2004 at 10:37 AM]
