=== Monday July 12, 2004 ===

I dream of life, and hardships

The wind cares not about such things that give us pause.  It lives with such courageousness, and fills the earth to it's full extent.  So can't we learn a lesson from the wind?  To live as fully as we can.  In time the wind can move full desserts.  And moving a desert may be impressive, but can we not learn something more from the wind?  In the company of rain and sun, the wind can move whole mountains.  And while I fully believe that one person can do so much in their life, one person joined by one person, joined by one person, can do so much more together!

It's true that one can change the world.  But I believe we have the power to change the world to such a greater extent than just one person alone ever could.  All it takes is unity, solidarity, many voices as one.  And while I'm sure this doesn't come as any great revelation to all of you reading this, sometimes the true power of many as one can get lost in the shuffle.  Don't ever let your voice be masked or filtered by another, but just as the elements work together to move mountains, so too do many voices... many different voices, come together to form a song.  Harmony, melody, background, foreground.

We can do so much.  We have the ability.  We have the potential.  We have the time.  We have the strength and determination.

And I'm so tired.  So I'm going to sleep.  Peace.

Shane

=== Sunday July 11, 2004 ===

Hunted in this world and the next...

I wrote this last night, from a sence of menace in the air that I felt.

+++

Tonight I am hunted as never before, either real or imagined.  Many playgrounds have their lines drawn on the ground; a call to order in an otherwise chaotic place and time.  I chose the hunted and I swear as sure as I could see her nakde soul through her windows, that the entire ocean was contained within her eyes... and the curve of her cheek all the gentle rounded beaches of the world.

And my choice brought turbulance in those eyes, and a darker curve to those slopes, and only a still and silent sadness remained.  A kind of sadness that can only be followed by the absence of all sound, and the drop of a single tear from an eye.  I chose the hunted, and she, my most beloved could do nothing but watch my spiral.  My sacrifice for her.

I fell into that place of thick jungle and resounding drums.  I fell into that place of awakened fear and no escape.  And though I still pay the price, to save her over again I'd endure twice as much five times over.  And tonight I find myself hunted as never before, sifted shadows from the corner of my eyes, and I know the nature of that shadow.  But I need not fear shadows for nothing exists without first the need for it to exist.

My existance fills a need, as does that shadow.  But it cannot ever take me, that is it's prison.  That is it's torment.  Mine is to be pursued by the intangible all my life, and it's is to never be able to catch me.  Our co-existance fills a need.

Oh, Shadow, you'll never catch me.

+++

You see, last night for the first time as clearly as this, I saw what appeared to be a shadow walk into a room of my house.  I went home this weekend, and I thought it was my brother playing tricks.  And, I've seen the flimsy 'out of the corner of your eyes' kinds of flickers of shadow before, and named them for tricks of light, but this seemed different.  I was convinced enough that it was a real person to go over and look into the room 'it' walked into.  Nothing.  No brother, no shadow, no nothing.  But it filled me with a sence of... well, not even really fear, but menace.  To see something so clearly and have it not be there.  It's just kind of spooky.  And spooky hasn't really happened to me in a really long time.

In any event, tonight I am back in my own home, and I'm going to sleep.

Peace,

Shane

[Posted 7/11/2004 at 9:12 PM]

=== Friday July 9, 2004 ===

The Beaten Path

So I begin along the beaten path, re-reading now, the 'Beat Spirit' by Mel Ash, and doing every single activity throughout the book.  Cover to cover.  I want to organize this a little as I go on, so I'm going to explain how the book is written.  There are chapters of sorts, that contain writings on different members of the Beat movement.  Each of these have several 'exercises' within based on the personality in question, and some of the things they did or wrote, or thought.  Exercises in freedom, nakedness of soul, and exhuberance of living.

I'm going to organize each author by Colour, and each time I do an exercise, the background colour is going to be based on the Author's chapter the exercise falls in.  For William S. Burroughs, who is the first chapter of the book, green is the background of choice.

So, onward.  And peace.

And anything but that kind of peace.  Anything but stagnation of spirit or belief.  I have a warrior friend with whom I haven't seen or spoken for some time, but it's really the time of warriors now.  Warriors of spirit, and conviction.  Warriors of belief, and action.  For my part, I'm fighting for my voice.  I'm fighting for my place. I'm fighting for everything I've never done.  And everything I have done.  And when I use the term Warrior, I don't personally mean bombs and guns.  It takes a warrior to stand up for what they believe in.  Despite those who rise against them.  I'm fighting for peace.  And a stop to idea that we should kill to stop killing.  We keep forgetting that nations have long memories, but people have short lives.

It's a hard line to walk, between one way and another.  But I believe in life.  And I don't believe in murder, or any kind.  And that's my own belief, but it's something I believe strongly.  Murder to stop murder is hypacritical, don't you think?

So my beat is beginning.  Exercises to come.  I'm ready for this.  I actually think I'm ready for the writing I'm about to write.  Love me or hate me, I have to be me, right?  I can't be a shadow all my life.

Peace to all of you,

Shane

[Posted 7/9/2004 at 10:19 PM]

=== Thursday July 8, 2004 ===

The Beat Movement

I've been reading about the beat movement lately.  Primarily, at least right now, I've been reading through a book called 'Beat Spirit' by Mel Ash.  It walks through many of the figures involved in the beat movement, and certain techniques used by each.  Phillosophies, thoughts, passions, failures, it speaks of a little but of everything.  I have to admit, I've been drinking it up since I found the book.  I next want to get books by many of the people I've read about now.  People I had previously only heard about, but never really thought to read.  It goes to show how much one can hear but shut out from the concscious mind.

William S. Burroughs, Allen Ginsber, Jack Kerouac, Gary Snyder, Michael Mclure.  All names I'm very much interested in reading.  The thing of it is, this book also touches on their methods, thoughts, and such as I've mentioned.  There are activities throughout the book to expand the mind, boundaries, or get rid of the boundaries altogether.  At the front of it all, it's about being yourself.  It's about being your true self.  About not giving in to the grind, though it grips us in it's steel jaws.  It's about looking above reality, to see the true reality.  Because really, it's about how we perceive it, not how it actually is.  As I've said before, my dreams are real to me, though they happen in my mind.  I live each moment, and remember much of them.  To me they are just as memories of days gone by.  So, for me, they are real.  They are part of my reality.

Maybe that's part of the reason the Beat Movement appeals to me.  Because I'm often vocal about being true to ourselves, about living life.  The only thing is, I often don't take the last step of actualization.  In that, I say the words, but don't breathe the breath.  Oh, I write myself near naked in front of those that may be reading, but is that enough?  I believe it's up to the individual.  The most important thing is to the self.  How does that expression go?

"Know thyself"

And you know, I absolutely fully believe it takes a lifetime.  And maybe a little more after that.  To know thyself, you have to live a complete liftetime.  Because everything usually seems clearer in hindsight.

Well, I think I'm going to go to bed now.  Work tomorrow.  Bwahaha.  It's ironic, after writing all this, that I'm going to work where I do.  But you know what?  Life is fucking beautiful, and I love every single moment of every single day.  Here's to mountain tops, and shouting from them!

Cheers,

Shane

[Posted 7/8/2004 at 11:18 PM]

=== Monday July 5, 2004 ===

Neverland and Peter Pan

I watched the movie called Peter Pan tonight.  The latest remake.  The one that told a story I remember reading in my storybook.  The one with the dark Mermaids, Princess Tigerlilly, clouds you can jump on, and flight like I've only had in dreams.  I don't know if it's just me, and I don't know if it's just at this time... just after a nice full moon, but the movie brought out the sadder emotions.  Lol.  I'm not even kidding!  It depressed me.  Don't get me wrong, I loved every minute of that movie, but it awoke other memories within me that I haven't had in a long time.  Memories of reading the book Peter Pan for the first time.  Memories of my yearning of Neverland probably much longer than I should have in my life.  But maybe not.  10 and 11 years old definately is not too old to be never wanting to grow up.  The thing of it is, I've held the dream of Neverland close to my heart for all my life.  My dreams take me there.  I've been to neverland.  I've been where stories are born.

And the thing of it is... I think I know what happens to Peter Pan.  He eventually grows up and starts to work Tech Support.  And the thing of it is... I'm desperately hoping to cheat the system.  I work in an office, and I do my job, and every moment I have for my own thoughts I'm back there again.  In neverland.  And while I was watching Peter Pan tonight, I thought of something else.  Neverland is like one person.  In constant conflict with themselves.  Peter Pan representing everything youthful.  Hopeful.  Carefree.  Crow!!!!!!  And Hook.  He represents growing up.  And they both represent the conflict every single one of us goes through in some form or another.

Growing up these days.  It seems to mean living in a world rushing to destroy itself.  Passively standing by while the people we elect democratically constantly tell us all the reasons they can't do most of what they said they would.  It means fingers over buttons.  It means blacking out the stars with, ironically, light.  It means haze, ruts that we all don't realize we're in, and just waiting for 'it' to happen around us.  Me inclusive.  And it all makes me want to climb the largest tree around and scream into the sky!  "I'm mad as hell and I'm not gonna take it any more!"

But these are my nighttime thoughts.  Life always smothers me in the mornings.  I used to wake up in the morning, and there was still the posibility of magic.  There was still the posibility that I would magically be transported into these other worlds I'd only read about.  Dreamed about.  I began to learn that one life was the waking life, and the other life was the lives lived in dreams, and they didn't tend to cross over too much after the age of 9 or 10.

And it's my words.  That's why I want to write words.  Words have power.  They have so much power.  And absolutely every one of us can evoke that power.  All you have to do is write who you are.  Without fear.  And I'll tell you why you can do it without fear.  Because anything you write, someone else has felt too in some similar way.  And I'm not trying to say that your lives are being lived by other people every day.  I'm trying to say we don't have to be afraid to write exactly who we are.  We're not alone in the thoughts that we thing.  The dreams that we long for.  At least I sure as hell hope not, or I'm in some trouble.

I guess I've just got a lot to say sometimes.  And hell, most of it's for my ears just as much as anyone who's reading this.

I used to want to become a merman and live under the ocean.  I wanted to be able to breathe under water.  To swim along the bottom of the ocean.  I wanted to be turned into a squirril while watching Sword in the Stone by Disney.  I wanted to get transported to Narnia after crawling into a cupboard.  I wanted to find myself in the Land of Fantasia from the Neverending Story.  I wanted to be the one to save the Little Mermaid from the original cartoon movie based on the original story by Hans Christian Anderson.  The one that ended badly for her.  I've always wanted the 'out of the ordinary' kind of life.  And I dont' know if I have it yet.  Not in the way I imagined.  I mean, when you wiegh the averages in life comparing every person to the next, I consider myself absolutely lucky as anything to have been born into Canada.  To have been born into a loving family, and to have met the people I have met so far in life.

So, it may not be magic entirely, but you know what?  I still look for the magic that exists around me.  There's a place in Toronto that I swear I saw in a dream.  It's the front yard of a Church down Young street near the Cemetary.  In the dream I was running from some kind of people, and ran into this same church yard, only it was edged by shrubs.  There were these druids working the land and plants in the yard.  One taught me about how to make the plants grow.  And I swear, when I first came across this churchyard in real life, I was simply amazed.  Now maybe it's not exactly the same, I dont' really know.  What I do know, is that it evoked so strongly the memory of that dream, that I had to take a deep breath, and just. Say. Wow.

So, as my rant draws to a close, I just want to say I love ya people. And I'm not even kidding right now.  Of those of you I read, even if I don't comment, I've most likely found myself caring about your lives as well.  Caring about the fact that you all exist as you do.  That you strive for what you strive for, love what you love, and grow as you grow.  And I think it's just because I plain love people.  They're all so damn different from each other.  And they all started out tiny little cells somewhere.  And I'm sure it really doesn't sound sincere, especially in such a mass scale as this, but I'm not even kidding.  Not even a little bit.  (And no, I haven't been dipping into the 'sauce').  I'm just me, remembering the things in life that bring magic back into my soul.  And love, loving friends and family around me, and feeling that love from friends in family in return, what is more magic than that.  Something so intangible, but stronger than anything tangible I've ever encountered.

Peace to you all,

Shane

[Posted 7/5/2004 at 10:26 PM]

=== Saturday July 3, 2004 ===

The City in Which I Live

[IMAGE: http://i.xanga.com/Stultiloquent/t/p1010023.jpg]

Well, these photographs you're about to see are from when I was on the company dinner-cruise around Centre Island in lake Ontario.  That Mercury filled body of water I touched upon briefly in yesterday's post.  It began with a rainstorm.  The cruise, much as my earliest memories.  And, also, as with most memories, it ended with a rainbow and a beautiful view.  This is Toronto Harbour.  I live just north of the lake down a street called Jarvis.  Of course, I move so often, I'm most likely not going to be there by the time you finish reading this post.

The cruise marked the first time I had ever seen a full rainbow.  And I'm not talking about the 'actual' thing a rainbow is.  A ring of light.  Since, I found out when I was young, that if I span around making a mist with the hose, that the rainbow went all around me.  It was kind of dissappointing to find out that there was no end to the rainbow.  Since I think one of my childhood dreams was to escape to the same place Rainbow bright lived.  They just seemed so happy there.... and hell, I wasn't an oblivious kid either.  I liked girls even at that age.  And I noticed that most of the Rainbow crew were female.  That's right.  What can I say?  So, what I mean in this case, is I saw the rainbow from one point on land reach another point on land.  The way a rainbow can only truly be seen when the sun is low in the sky.  At least, from what I gather.

[IMAGE: http://i.xanga.com/Stultiloquent/p1010021.jpg][IMAGE: http://i.xanga.com/Stultiloquent/p1010020.jpg]
[IMAGE: http://i.xanga.com/Stultiloquent/p1010019.jpg][IMAGE: http://i.xanga.com/Stultiloquent/p1010018.jpg]

So there you have it.  A rainbow.  My first full rainbow.  On a night that marks just over a year at this company.  I'm still growing within the company too.  Except, the more I plant my roots someplace, the more I want to fly away.  Maybe a different city.  Force myself to change the way I look at life.  Or rather, change the way I look at myself.  And I'm definately not complaining about the job, even though having pager seems to bring that question to the front.

And to you, I understand what it is to be on call now.  I understand that little bit more.

So now I'm going back to work on some issue I have no real idea to what is going wrong.  Of all 6 pages today, this one had to come along.  Every other page resulted in a resolved issue after about 10 minutes.  This one has been ongoing for some time.  In fact, it was found out during the week, but nobody bothered to dig deeper into the issue, so of course they call again on the weekend because their stores aren't processing credit properly.  No credit means no money, and that means problems.

I swear.  It's a full moon, and I'm here thinking about people I used to talk to.  During full moons or otherwise.  And how I'd much rather be talking to people I care about than working pager.  And the moon, while usually bringing out the wolf in me, seems to be only bringing out the howl in me.  Or, rather, the pager's bringing out the howl.  The Moon.  I can't blame her.  Never figured out yet if it was she pursuing the sun, or the sun pursuing her though.

We'll see who catches who first.

But that's crazy talk, and some customer needs my help.

Somewhere, there is a pager going off.  Till next time, adieu,

Shane

[Posted 7/3/2004 at 10:4 PM]

=== Thursday July 1, 2004 ===

Damnit.

Damnit, damnit, damnit.

I feel like I'm trying to balance on some freaky tightrope with no net, and no view of whatever I'm hanging above.  It doesn't help that I'm on pager this week.  Crazy pager beeping.  And it's funny, but having pager constantly makes me question why the hell I'm doing this.  Why I care even a little bit about money.  About making money.

In my wildest dreams it doesn't exist.  Hell, in all my dreams it doesn't exist.  Most of my dreams take place in some kind of post-apocalyptic world where the few survivors are trying to do just that.  Survive.  My other dreams are more fantastical, or don't even touch upon the thought of money.

Waking up is never easy.

And it doesn't help that I sometimes feel I'm about 'this' close to being one of those people who shuts themselves away from the 'civilized' world in search of inner peace.  Except, I like people, just about as much as I fear meeting 'new' people.  It's a crazy vicious cycle.

I am water.  The path of least resistance.  That's usually me.  Except I'm stubborn as both my parents combined.  And I can't stand failure in myself.  I really and truly can't.  And now, I think, this marks the first time I've ever commited that to the written word, or even spoken it.  It's not like it should be a revelation or anything to me, only it is.  I don't think I can stand failure.  It's why I'm so freaking terrified of any kind of lasting decision.  You make a decision, and there's a chance of failure.  I'm always playing chess with my life.  Only, instead of moving the pieces, I'm thinking ahead to damn much.

And it's funny, but I tend to gravitate towards leadership in most situations.  I'm often indecisive, but in a necessary situation, I'm a leader in a pinch.

I think the word amorphous fits me.  And that drives me crazy.  Lacking shape.  Because, now another fear is creeping up.  My fear of failure has halted me often to indecision.  Except now, at this point in my life, if I don't start making lasting decisions, my indicisiveness will be the cause of my failure.  My failure to truly live how I want to live.

You can't freaking please everyone in life.  And this next thought goes along with my thought that if I'm thinking it, someone else must be to.  If I try to at least make myself truly happy, lord knows I'll probably make some other people happy along the way.

*peace*.  Peace.  My mind is feeling ravaged right now.  Three pages in three hours and now sweet, sweet sleep.  Before Friday and then a page filled weekend.  Oh lordy, I can't wait until my vacation in August.  North to isolation for a week or so.  Stars the way they should be seen, and water so clean you can at least put yourself in it without getting mercury poisoning.

The world as it is... I tell ya.  I'm on the edge of my seat to see what happens next.  Better than the soaps.  That's for damn sure.

Peace to you all.

Shane

[Posted 7/1/2004 at 10:26 PM]

=== Tuesday August 31, 2004 ===

[IMAGE: http://i.xanga.com/Stultiloquent/t/IMG_0009.JPG]

This is my space at work.  It's where I put away such things as most of my dreams and take out my thinking cap.  It's where everything tends to fade and blur and blend.  Except I find ways to escape, even here.  I have origami, I have two pictures on the wall.  I have a directory filled with whatever writing I feel I should write from time to time.  I havea pen and post it notes.  I'm in control of my mind and my thoughts for most of the workday, but sometimes I have to relent to maintain that control.  Sometimes I need to close my eyes, take a breath, and take myself away from this.  I can go to the ocean and swim.  Ride the waves, carried by the wind.  Or dive, dive, dive.  I belong under water.  It's where I'm most at home.

+++

He stared at the bed, and the sleeping man burried under the hospital restraints and pristine sheets.  He could feel darkness inside, even from 5 feet away.  Closing his eyes, he reached out and locked on to the darkness, pulling silently with his mind.  Slowly, the thing seeped out of the sleeping figure and into him as he fought to absorb that darkness.  It's the only way. He thought to himself.  Healing wasn't as miraculous as some thought.  Everything had a price.  To heal; to heal emotionally or mentaly, one had to take in the pain.  To rid people of their demons, one had to draw them through themselves first before passing them to the void.  And some people... such pain they could feel.  He stood, trembling as the darkness slipped through his soul, trying to take root.  You have no power over me.  I have power over myself.  You have no power over me.  I have power over myself. A silent mantra against the shadows.  A muttered prayer of identity against the onslaught of emotion, pain, and the demon from which they sprouted.  He fell to his knees crying out. "Yevesh!" He fell to his knees as the demon passed through him to the void.  Except, as everything had a price, and there always remained a piece of that darkness within him.  Such healing as this required such a price.  He pulled himself up with the help of a nearby chair and slowly walked out of room 208.  At least this time, again he was still himself.

+++

Back to work, back to that desk and all the things that go with that.  Everything does have a price.  So too does living in Toronto.

Ciao for now,

Shane

[Posted 8/31/2004 at 3:35 PM]

=== Monday August 30, 2004 ===

[IMAGE: http://i.xanga.com/Stultiloquent/t/Toronto%20and%20Work%2020040802%20034.jpg]

An open ice-cream truck just sitting there.  This would have been my wildest dream one time in my childhood.  Now it's just something interesting on the way to work I got to snap a picture of.  You can see the chilled fog escaping through the door.  I love the vivid blue of the truck.

I'm still around.  Commenting only sporadically, but my mind is running a mile a minute.  I started working from 11-7 again.  But I'm tired right now.  I need to try to force myself to stay awake for some time now, because I don't want to wake up 3 hours before work.  I want to sleep until at least 9:30.

I started writing a short story or a novel.  It's based on a dream I had... or inspired from, rather.  I don't want to do more than mention even slightly.  In fact, I may post only pictures and brief poems or words for the next little while.  I'm entering a 'phase' I think.  A man of little words phase.

+++

I missed her as soon as I saw the bus barrel away.  I missed her the second her hand left my own and she climbed the steps of the bus.  I missed her the moment I walked with her through the cold and wind, using only each other to stay warm.  I missed her the moment I met her, knowing that she'd go away, knowing that I'd go away as well.  I missed her the moment I heard her voice.  And I've loved her ever since.  On fire.  The Autumn reminds me of her.  And certain songs.  And the full moon that reigns above tonight.  They all light the way.

+++

G'night,

Shane

[Posted 8/30/2004 at 11:13 PM]

=== Saturday August 28, 2004 ===

[IMAGE: http://i.xanga.com/Stultiloquent/t/perfect%20as%20is%20subway.jpg]

I like the colour red.  Not on it's own, but in combination with other colours.  And I don't like it as much except when brilliantly red.  The kind of red you can't despute is not red.  The kind of red that can't be called 'rust' or 'burgundy' or 'fuchia'.  Red that isn't afraid to be exactly what it is.  Absolutely, utterly, without hestitation, red.  The fact of the matter is, I like most colours that don't shirk their identities.  My favourite colour is blue, but still, I find myself drawn to certain colours at certain times.  Maybe it's just one of those things like tastebuds.  Change with age.

And it isn't age that changes us so much as the experiences we find to fill in the years, hours, days.  The stories people tell us add to that, and compound, and grow into our own experiences as well.  I'm the sum of my parts, but also the sum of the parts that others have shared with me.  Passions, poetics, pouts, and priorities.  Something shared is something... something.

It's 1:18, and I haven't been up this late in a while.  At least, I don't think I have.  I've been kind of out of it lately.  Talking to myself at night, trying to sort 'things' out.  They're night demons, because they're gone by sunrise.  They're my demons because they know me better than I know myself.  And they're demons because they force me to look at even those things about myself and life that I'd almost rather ignore or never remember.

I have absolutely no stress tonight.  None.  It feels absolutely incredible.  I know that when I wake up tomorrow, wihtout the aid of an alarm clock, I can make my way to the bus terminal to catch a bus into my hometown.  Visit with family and a friend, and maybe if the mood strikes me head into a bar for a while with said friend.  The key point here is that it doesn't really matter how this weekend turns out.  I just don't care how it turns out.  It is going to be a weekend of absolutely as little stress as possible.  Because my mind is steering me towards that kind of revelation.  Life is only as stressfull as you make it.

I guess, what I'm trying to say is that I feel good.  There's lots I have to do in the next few months, but I feel good.  Tonight, this week, tomorrow as well, I reckon I'll continue to feel good.  Not to mention my room is again reaching that state of cleanliness that allows my mind to be as free of clutter as my newly discovered carpeted floor!

I really am tired though, but quite honestly, as good as I do feel right at this moment, those demons have been hounding me at night.  This past week it's been more of a struggle of life and what comes after.  I usually firmly believe that there is something after death.  In fact, it IS what I believe.  Except, sometimes I have doubts.  Then, I discuss the alternatives with myself.  Or argue with the demons on my back.  I usually win in the end.  It's hard to argue uncertainties with more uncertanties to back you up.  The thing is, even though I choose to believe that there is something after we leave the physical world, I don't know what it's like.  So, even on a good day, when I absolutely have faith in something after death, I often fear what exactly it might be like.

But I don't mean to get bogged down tonight with all that mud.  I feel good.  I'm going to wish you all sweet dreams...

Which brings me to a crazy dream I had last night.  An interesting one, to say the least.  We'll see what I'm trying to tell myself in that soon enough.  For now, g'night, and may your own demons leave you alone for a good long while.

Peace,

Shane

[Posted 8/28/2004 at 1:28 AM]

=== Tuesday August 24, 2004 ===

More's the Fool

I am often very much a fool.  I do foolish things.  I've made more than my share of stupid decisions in life.  It's easy to look back and point them all out.  Each single moment that has changed our paths in ways we always wondered about.  Ways that might have gone differently.  So I call myself a fool.  However, when going through this cycle of thought, the one that always follows that certain song, smell, or person that sets us on that spiral.  You know, they call them triggers sometimes.  They call them triggers, and make some kind of disorder out of them.  I know what a trigger is, I know how I feel after I'm set off.  I know that it's like walking through shadows.  You grasp at things and you hit nothing.  You reach and reach all around, and in the end you end up wrapping those reaching arms around yourself.  Protecting yourself from your own thoughts.  Or trying to.  But sometimes they just don't stop.  Drowning in memories, whispers, half formed paths, and promises.  Wishes too.

So I say I'm a fool.  Aha.  But then, always when I'm not there I think even more.  When I'm not among those shadows or dark places.  When I'm not sitting with my hand on the wall wishing I could just pass through.  When I'm not in that state of wanting so desperately to know.  Anything!  To know anything for certain.  To know if that kiss was real.  To know if that person was real.  To know if the sun truly will rise for us tomorrow.

It's when I'm not there that I think differently.  So very differently.  All those 'stupid' decisions we've made in life.  They've got at least an equal ammount of great decisions.  For all those shadows of doubt, and paths unwalked, there are others that have been explored.  There are places that aren't so dark.  And it's then that the power of choice gains a different light.  Yes, we all make bad choices, and sometimes we start thinking in circles, in that dark place where the mind broods, screams, and otherwise struggles.  But choice is the word.  Choice.  We can't always know (almost never) where a choice will truly take us.  It's only in the hindsight that we see so clearly.

I learned that in grade 10, but never applied it to self analysis.  "Hindsight is 20/20" Ms. Craven said.  So, take that.  Take it and use it maybe.  You can never know, not ever, where a path will take you.  You can spend years pondering outcomes and possibly never hit upon the right one.  You might think you have it, and it's changed by something as simple as a spring shower.  A bump in the road.  Anything at all.

Butterflies in Africa causing hurricanes on the East Coast.

And I know it's cyclical.  I know it always comes in circles.  The agony and the ecstacy.  And I fully believe there are more people that know exactly what I'm talking about than might ever tell in the 'real' world.  I fully believe that we all sometimes get to that place where we just think "What the fuck.  What the hell am I doing here.  This isn't where I thought I'd be."  Or something as simple as "I remember".  Those two words can bring so many things to the mind.

But hey, this is just another post.  I still don't know what the hell I'm doing here.  I don't even know if I'll keep focusing on the 'what' anymore so much as try to start just doing it in the firstplace.  You have to start walking if you expect to ever get anywhere.

So, I'll tell you what I'm going to do.  I'm going to walk into the bathroom, have a shower, and then I'm going to walk back into my bedroom and sleep.  Because right now, that's where I want to go.  Hell, I deserve to sleep.

It's been that kind of day.  I hope you all have sweet dreams,

Peace,

Shane

[Posted 8/24/2004 at 11:22 PM]

=== Thursday August 19, 2004 ===

[IMAGE: http://i.xanga.com/Stultiloquent/img_0467.jpg]

I've always and unconditionally been water
but I've never kissed the sky
though my waves try
and try, and try.

I felt the tide, to her moon's push
her influence apparent
in my stormy blue-green surges
reaching for land
falling short on
a sand and rock prison

I've always and unconditionally been water
but she is the sky that I'll never touch
though my waves try,
and try, and try.

+++

Shane

=== Sunday August 15, 2004 ===

Home again, home again, jiggedy jig.

Well, I'm back from a week and a half vacation up north.  Photo's forthcoming.  I just have to recharge my batteries at work tomorrow.  They're dead in my camera.

I had a good time, not a long time, and the sun certainly didn't shine every day!

But, the key phrase there is good time.  I enjoyed my time away from work.  Time to think, to slow down, to take pictures, and to doodle and write.  So much has happened, and is happening to me at work, home, everywhere.  So many choices I have to make soon.  Larger directional choices.  With work is coming the funds to either go to school, travel europe, buy a condo (downpayment) or start a company, or cycle across canada, or any number of paths.

Oh, I know, I talk of them often.  So many paths.  Blah blah blah.  You're right.  Enough for now.  I'm back from vacation, and I'm ready for work.  We'll see where it takes me tomorrow.

Heck, my resolve in certain futures may just grow with the moon.  I always get this way when the moon fades into it's new-moon phase.

Anyway, I'm off to sleep, dream, and slip into rat-race mode once again.

Bad Shane.  Bad.  Rat-race mode's gonna kill you one of these days.  I'm still looking for a way to cheat the system.  Get rat-race money without rat-race worries, but I fear the worries have a way of sticking around.  That's okay, maybe I can still create a hermitage somewhere.  Party at my hermitage.  Everyone's invited!  I know, a little odd for a hermit... maybe I'm just more a hippie at heart.

Damn the man.

Damn.

I'm tired.

Sweet dreams.Shane

=== Monday August 2, 2004 ===

The One Thing

We could talk numbers all day
you and I
and be no closer to the end
than we were a thousand hours ago
and a hundred miles away

we could talk arithmatic all night
you and I
and take no count of hours or minutes
passing by the millions, year in
and year as always, out

we could talk quantitative
you and I
but we'd forget the in-between
when the sky kisses the ground
and we kiss each other

+++

Shane

=== Monday August 2, 2004 ===

There is no pain that is not from my mind created (Or, for those of you who dislike the double negatives in that... All pain stems from the mind)

By this I mean, before we can feel pain, it must first travel to and be processed by the brain.  This further means, that by learning to control our minds, we can prevent ourselves from feeling pain.  But I think it has a kryptonite... and I think that kryptonite is called PAGER!!!

One more night of Pager.  After tonight.  I mean, I have pager on Monday night as well, being as tomorrow's a holiday, and nobody will be coming in to work tomorrow to liberate me from the pager.  We like to compare pager with the ring that Frodo had to bear.  It's a heavy burden.  And I swear, I always think about 'life' when I have the pager.  There's so many things I want to do.  Places I want to visit.  People I know are out there that I want to meet, even if I don't know them yet.  And for the love of whatever you believe in, I don't want to be 80 writing these very same words but in regret rather than yearning.

I was standing at the sink only 30 minutes ago, transfixed by the stream of water coming from the faucet after my simply turning the tap.  Transfixed.  All of a sudden, there was this stream of cold water pouring into my cupped hands.  I just stared at it pooling there, trying to comprehend the enormity of even something as simple as running water.  Think about this.  Is there anyone else out there that feels that?  Awe.  I'm in awe of all the things we have available to us.  Running, cold, water.  Or, running hot water if we so desire.

I can, at any moment I chose, go to a sink in this apartment, and turn on a tap.  At that moment, water will begin pouring into the sink.  If I'm thirsty (and brave) I can drink the water coming forth.  How can I not be in awe of even a simple thing as running water.  Even providing that we had running water in cities even a few thousand years ago I think.  Well, however long ago Rome housed an idealistic idea enforced by many a power hungry individual.  But then again, ancient history, however interesting to me, is not my forte.

This is now.  This is me turning on a light and being in awe.  Just think, every once and a while, what has gone on in history, in our parents lives, or our parent's parents... to make this all happen.  Wars fought for land, industry, ideas, power.  We live the way we do now, because of everything happening exactly as it did every step of the way through history.  And when I think of that, it is easy to be horrified.  War after war of progress to give these things to us, or to take them away.

It's a times like these I know full well I'm just another idealist.  That my hopes for the world are just those.  But I am going to enjoy every second of this life that I have.  And appreciate every little thing.  Today, I am alive, and living where I am because a war was fought in and around these lands.  I'm Canadian because my family's families came here from Europe to find something, or run from something else.  A new start maybe, a clean slate.  An escape from memories, or just opportunity.  I'm here because someone took a first step.  Someone built a first fire.  Someone dreamed.  Someone believed in something that didn't exist at the time.

All these things that we coexist with in our daily lives, are things that never existed before.  Not as they do now.  It takes a dream, a desire, and a whole hell of a lot of determination to make things happen like that.  To take something old, or two things old, and make one thing new.

That's one reason I love art.  I believe in art.  It brings our minds places we might not have gone.  Forces us to think new thoughts, or rethink old ones.  Art and science most definately go together.  Both are born of dreams.  Both are born of soul.

Needless to say, I'm tired still... and I want to get to and through tomorrow as swiftly as possible.  Sweet dreams guys, and don't forget to remember them in the morning.  At least for a little while.  The stuff of reality was once the stuff of dreams first.  Remember that!  And then, perhaps, take that first step towards something you have been hesitating on or with.  It won't hurt, not in the end.  Not at 80 when you can look back and say, yes, I did that.  Nobody can say I didn't.
Dare to dream.Peace,Shane

[Posted 8/2/2004 at 12:2 AM]

the intuitive and psychic realms. This is the
stuff dreams are made on. And like dreams the
imagery we find here may inspire us or torment
us. Understanding the moon requires looking
within. Our own bodily rhythms are echoed in
this luminary that circles the earth every
month and reflects the sun in its progress.

and lead you towards insight. The Moon is a
force that has legends attached to it. It
carries with it both romance and insanity.
Moonlight reveals itself as an illusion and it
is only those willing to work with the force of
dreams that are able to withstand this
reflective light. Image from: Stevee Postman.

=== Sunday September 26, 2004 ===

Preventative Measures
or
The way I built a fence around my world.

I'm afriad this
blog is entering protected mode.  It's entering protected mode for
many reasons.  These reasons do not include trying to prevent
anyone from my 'real' life world from reading these words.  I wish
I could leave these words absolutely unprotected, all my poetry,
thoughts and dreams.  The fact is, I someday want to publish what
I have.  I really, really do.  I've been looking back and
since 2000 when I first started writing here, I've got a lot of
material.  Both poetry and prose.  Now, provided I can bring
myself to sort the wheat from the chaff in all this material, I think I
have a good shot at publishing.  I've just never begun taking
steps to get me to that place.  One thing I fear is one day
picking up a book and seeing my words starting back at me with
another's name attributed to them.  I am the words I write, for me
there is no distinction.  I bleed into my poems like watercolour
on thick, fibrous paper.  There is a piece of me in every single
letter.

So, I believe
it's something I must do, to protect myself for now and in the
future.  I'm going to go through my subscriptions and subscribers
and add people to the protected list.  If you find yourself not on
this list and wish to be, please leave a comment to this post.
For those who have never read me before, I've kept a few posts open
below.  A sampling of my writing, to help anyone who may stumble
along decide if they do want to be added to my protected list.

Peace to you all,

Shane

[Posted 9/26/2004 at 8:24 PM]

=== Saturday September 25, 2004 ===

Hazmat and Hyacinth (Poem 8)

Sometimes a buffer is necessary
to see this through to spring
the long standing ovation of the soul
hidden by fog and mist
acid rain, and forest fires
winter winds, and most of all
the frost, come morning.

Sometimes I need to see you
through your thicker skin
beneath your divine protection
and into the heart of the girl become woman
become frown, become smile.

It's your lips I want, but upward,
it's your eyes I want, with lines.
A crinkle for laughter,
wrought with gentle, playful years.

You are poetry; bittersweet and beautiful
a sunrise breaking waves
standing in for the moon, you soar higher
you sing louder.
force of nature, you.

You are my contemplation, and my silence.
The place my mind wanders to at night,
when the sky is not enough, even for me.
When the Moon in all her glory,
can't captivate me as you can.

It's madness, it's sanity, it's all in-between
it's the way you see into my eyes seeing into yours
and knowledge is there!
Our eyes, meet and wisdom follows
how could it take as long as an age
and two lifetimes to get here?

Some lessons worth learning,
becoming ourselves,
that's why, that's the reason.
All things in their season.

This season is ours.

+++

Shane
[Posted 9/25/2004 at 12:40 AM]

=== Tuesday September 21, 2004 ===

Speak to Me

"am I alive, or thoughts that drift away
does summer come for everyone
can humans do what prophets say"

we drifted, you and I
long before the winter wind
swept us into spring
and hollow summers

waiting for that perfect moment
to rip us from our groove
but perfect moments never come
and waiting takes forever

we cannot wait forever

"and if I die before I learn to speak
can money pay for all the days
I've lived awake, but half asleep"

and Autumn takes my breath away
there are no words
no desire greater than to see
the sun and the ocean become one
as a harvest moon rises
and the night awaken a singing in the soul

speak to me now
forever can wait.

+++

Shane

(Italicized quotations from "Standing outside a broken phonebooth with money in my hand" by The Primitive Radio Gods.  A song that never fails to give me goosebumps, nor ever fails to remind me that life has to be lived every day.  That waiting isn't an option.  You build up your world, your career, you get your money in your pocket and realize that maybe there were some things in life that slipped away because of it.)

Peace

=== Monday September 13, 2004 ===

you are splashes of colour
amidst the shades of grey in life
fiery red, feisty,
ferociously yourself

you watch my blues
stark contrast to your hues
and we laugh because
the world isn't ready for us

+++++

i live for this, a learning curve
the revelations people bring
to the world, to themselves,

to me

i live for finding, seeking,
and you are worth understanding

+++++

Autumn's reds, alive
I feel the pulse, it's Gaia
Breathe, you are a part

+++++

Peace,

Shane

=== Thursday September 9, 2004 ===

[IMAGE: http://i.xanga.com/Stultiloquent/t/Guardian.jpg]

Containers

I like containers.  I like they way the can be empty, or contain something.  I've always loved wooden boxes, or anything with a lid.  The mystery of what could be inside, or what could potentially be stored within just gets to me.  Compartments for this, compartments for that.

I like talking with people, opening those compartments in others and revealing that which I myself, compartmentalize.  With me the same topics may come up again and again, but maybe it's because at certain times I'm cleaning out those same containers within myself.  Our minds make associations that we travel along.  Our minds work largely with association.  This triggers that.  So on and so on.  Again, since it's currently the fall, certain trees give off a smell that reminds me of Coniston.  It reminds me of my Grandmother's house and the tree that used to reside in the backyard, perilously close to the shed also in the backyard.

My Grandmother isn't doing so well right now.  She's in a great deal of pain, pain that all of us thought had finally been taken care of by certain medication.  She has some kind of polymuscularsomething or other.  I'm not certain of the name, but what I am certain of is that on top of that problem with pain, she's an almost 90 year old woman living on her own.  Previously by her own choice.  I love my grandmother, and I hate that she's in pain.  I hate that all the memories I have of her will be what remains when she is gone.  That one day I will not be able to surprise her with a visit as I have a few times this year.  What I love... what I love is that I was able to take time this year to surprise her on a few occasions.  To hear her talk of her life.  Her childhood, her parents, her house before the house she lives in now.  Her family's house.  A house on a hill.  And also of my Father and my uncles.  When they were younger, and of my Grandfather of whom I remember very little save the few quarters I got from him the last time he visited us coming back from Florida.

The thing is, I guess I don't mean for this to be a kind of depressing post.  It's just something that is there right now, in my mind and I'm certain in the minds of my family and her friends.  (Of which she has many).  She is a remarkable woman, and definately does not deserve any of the pain she currently feels.  I hope and pray that her body accepts and utilizes the medication that it is being given.  I want nothing more than to have many more years of her in this world with all of us.  I wish more than anything that any children I will have in this life were here right now.  So they can meet her.  I'm just glad that my memories are as vivid as they are, and that I have the ability to relay memories on paper.

I think very soon I'm going to be continuing the series I started on my Grandmother and her house.  Pictures not just of the street and outside of the house, but pictures and stories of within.  And of her.  In any event, my lunch break is just about over and I need to turn my mind to more immidiate issues.

Peace and Longevity,

Shane

[Posted 9/9/2004 at 4:19 PM]

=== Monday September 6, 2004 ===

The wavelength of life is increasing it's frequency

The highs and lows of life, it just seems to me that they are happening in a much quicker succession than previously.

I'm so out of words right now it's not funny, and I have heaps of pictures I want to post here but can't work up the initiative to actually upload to Xanga.

In fact, I'm surprised that I'm typing even these few words right now.  And I don't even think it's depression at all, it's more a lack of any kind of motivation whatsoever.  Money doesn't motivate me.  Personal gain doesn't really motivate me.  All my life no matter what I'm doing, I've always sought the most efficient way of doing something, so I wouldn't have to do it for as long or as often.  I'm motivated by dreams when I actually write, but when I start to write the dreams into the page I find that they're harder to keep ahold of than I thought.  I try even to write the images down and they slip away.  I'm so frustrated that I can feel and see something so completely in my head but be unable to relate that to anybody else except through them being right there in front of me at the time.  Because all the words I've ever written pale in comparison to the actual emotion of the events.  They grow stale on the page and I wonder if the only way to every get these things across to anyone else would be for them to see me remembering those said moments.  See me relating my stories and remembering.  See the way my face changes, my eyes.  My mouth, and any kind of body language.

Then I realize that I feel so uncomfortable around most people that I'd be unable to relate that kind of passion to anybody I didn't know and cherish.  And while I cherish a few people, they remain just that.  A few people.

So that leaves me with just words, and mabey spoken voice if I decide to start posting some of my words vocally.  I've thought about that, except it still misses the body language.  Words have power, but I think the way of delivering the words is just as important.  I love poetry because they can be as free from form as you choose, or they can be held by form but cry against it all the while.  Or they can be purely form, with the passion somewhat caged, but only to cause the reader to think just a little more... and maybe read just a little into the words.

Words have power, but so does movement.  Action.  So do images on a page.  So do voices.  Some of the conversations I've had with people in my life would be the best poems.  Human poetry.  You know, you can even think of us as being the words.  We're words alive.  What we do, how we act, the way two people look at each other across the street while waiting for the 'walk' signal.  It's all poetry.  The way one person charges down the street aware only of themselves and not even noticing how many people have to get out of 'their' way.  And others who walk along, staring at the sidewalk all the while.  One foot after the other, like they were walking their last walk.

Sometimes I'm just so frustrated with words.  No matter how much I may ever get to master words on the page, in person my words are always full of lead.  Unless you know me and I know you.  Unless you challenge me to be comfortable.  Dare me to it.  I don't know why I'm like that.  I really don't.  I was one of the most outgoing people when I was younger.  Until I moved back to Canada.  11 years old, new school, new country, and new peers.

I think that often dreams fade so that they can never be captured but in the heart.  And only given to others who share our hearts with us.  Those people who know us and cherish us as much as we cherish them.

It's just a thought as I get ready to sleep.  It's a half-moon tonight... so I'm only half crazy.

Peace,Shane

=== Thursday September 2, 2004 ===

[IMAGE: http://i.xanga.com/Stultiloquent/t/IMG_0014.JPG]

New and Old, so I've been told, It's all the same to me

From right to left, the books I've brought to work, and just left here.  Besides, I like to show people parts of my personality that don't usually come out at work.  The kind that likes Folklore from around the world, old books, and English Breakfast Tea.

Folktales from Inda - A book filled with folktales from Inda.  I know, you were expecting a book with that kind of title to hold limricks from Ireland.

The Psychoanalysis of Dreams - A book I haven't touched yet.  It's kind of dated, but I'm interested in what it has to say. Again, title self explanatory.

A Man for All Seasons - A play by Robert Bolt.  About a man who adheres to his principles and ideals, no matter what the cost.  Admirable, maybe, but there's been at least one time in my life that adhering to certain principles has been the absolute wrong thing for me to do.

Personal Best - A collection of Thirty Australian authors' chosen best short stories.

Tables of Houses - A collection of latitude and longitudes of something or other to do with the Rosicrucian Fellowship.  I haven't done much research on them, but I bought the book at an old used book store.  And, since I love old books, like this one.  Plus, blue's my favourite colour anyhow.

The Poetical Works of John Milton - Title self explanatory here.  Again, a used book store is where I purchased this one.  In the front cover is the following writing... which is why I love buying old books. "Mr E. Penfold, Paris Ont. Nov. 20th 1869".  Did I mention I love old books?  I love old books.  And this one's certainly old.

Ship of Magic, then Fool's Errand - Robin Hobb's books.  Two of them anyhow, fantasy books, excellently written.

Exiles - A book by Melanie Rawn... haven't read this oe yet.  And looking to my left, it's no longer at my desk either.  I'm sure I'll get to it.

Anyhow, I really need to get back to work now.  I'll talk to you all another time.

Peace,

Shane

=== Thursday October 28, 2004 ===

Dreams, Reality, and the difference between the two...

Hi Guys.  I just wanted to post a link to another page I have where I exclusively write my dreams and thoughts on dreams down.  I figure, since you're all on my protected list, I can post it here as you're all able to read these words because I trust y'all.  It's AshenFrae .  I created it because I post poetry here, and other thoughts.  I wanted a place specifically for my dreams.  I like to analize my dreams.  I like to write things on my dreams, and I like to hear about other peoples dreams too.  I guess I'm just plum fascinated with dreams in general.  So, you're all welcome to stop in if your'e in to that kind of thing.  One thing I've learned is that there are some people who share my love of dreams, and others who could care less. :-)  That page is definately for the type of person who is interested in that sort of thing.

Peace to you all,

Shane

=== Sunday October 24, 2004 ===

"That's just the way it is..."

I've been thinking lately, and even more just now as my Grandmother rests in a hospital for the night (at least), that I really do believe.  When it comes down to it, I absolutely believe in everything insubstantial, immaterial, and mysterious about the world and universe we live in.  As my Grandmother lies with a possible Pneumonia, I know without a doubt, that it's all irrefutably okay in the end.  And while my current lack of overly sad emotion is bothering me more than just a little bit right now, I have a feeling it's because of the potential strength in my belief that life most certainly does not end after we take our last breath.  And that thought, comforts me a little.

Where my Grandmother is at right now.  In her last years, days, who knows how long, it's that time where she's in the process of her final winding down.  And it is sad.  That her laughing face, her loving smile, and her interest in people... will all be gone.  Yes, that does make me sad... but I find myself mostly unemotional about the whole thing.  Like I'm accepting this as a rite of passage.  I know that some things in life just are.  And for all our struggling still remain as they are.  We can delay floods, prolong life, cure some sicknesses, reach the moon and someday stars, but we must move on one day from all of this.  From this particular perspective.  As much as I love the life I'm living, I believe it's going to be okay.  I really and truly do.

And yes, it may just be that my present apathy is a defence mechanism.  I've often been unemotional at funerals.  Had my first one before I was 6 I believe.  An uncle I didn't really know.  I played hide and seek with some other kids, and thoroughly enjoyed the candy dishes in various locations around the showing place.  Not to mention the fact I got to see much of my family.  And I do love my family.  Only two deaths have seriously affected my thought processes, and emotions to such a great extent.  To a life-changing extent.  One was my cousin Shawn.  With whom I share the initials SDF.  The other was a friend I hadn't spoken to for 3 years.  Just someone who I once had the potential to be really good friends with.  Her name was Mel.  She was truly a wonderful person.

So, self defence mechanism or not, I do believe in more than this.  Life teaches many things, it brings us both pain and pleasure unlike anything I'm sure we'll ever have to face again.  It presents powerful emotion and thought processes.  It provides unimaginable uncertainty of anything.  It almost seems like a test in that regard.  When almost nothing is certain.  What else is left?  Just belief in something.  Even something as simple as the sun rising tomorrow.  Oh, science can say it's a certainty.  But you truly never know what will happen.  By everything I hold dear, I do so very much love life.  And nothing in this world that can be touched or bought or acquired, none of it even comes close to the value I place on the people that populate it.  We're all connected, and it's just there's so damn much interference in this life.  So embrace each other in any way you can, and enjoy the ride.

Grandma, you know I'm there with as much spirit and energy as I can give.  May your pain be as slight as possible and your dreams as captivating as they always seem to be.

Love,Shane Denis Fera

[Posted 10/24/2004 at 9:10 PM]

=== Thursday October 21, 2004 ===

"'Round here, we always stay up late..."

It's been quite a while since I last posted.  Well, by my recent standards of writing on Xanga.  I've been a little emotionally dry lately.  As if my brain is releasing some chemical to just cut out the emotions I might feel.  I feel dull, uncreative, unmotivated, and blah.  Oh that's right folks, I am in a state of blah.  Which makes it both a noun, as well as an adjective.  I guess a full moon is coming soon.  And Halloween to boot.  I like that part of the year.  You know, it's been blah, and wierd too.  More often these days I'm hit with that sense of 'oddness' with the world.  You know, where you take a breath, and just stare around because suddenly it's as if the world around you has taken on this 'unreality' to it.  Kind of like a light filter.  Like everything is being filtered through something.

I'm also not feeling very well right now.  I guess it's contributing to my mood.  The fact that I can sometimes have hypocondriac tendancies.  The thing of it is, despite the fact I am a little fearful about when I'm feeling this crappy, I have this innate unwillingness to go to a doctor.  I don't like going to those places that have the power to tell me things look good or things look bad.  Shite.  I guess it's all contributing to my mood.  Right now it hurts if I breathe out too far.  On the left side of my chestbone.  And my throat has this coating that makes it difficult to eat.  And painful to swallow at all.  And I don't mean to complain, except all these are things I think I just need to write to get out of my system.

This undeniable state of blahness.  And last night was dreamless, whilst the dream a night before was filled with people who weren't what they appeared.  Some kind of being wearing the 'faces' so to speak, of friends of mine, and family.  And I'm almost certain this is some kind of psychhological onionskin peeling away with recent events within my usually stable world.  It's calmed down though, but my mind likes to make stories out of things while I sleep.  To form everything together into plots so it makes some kind of sense.  Can't I just have an absolutely nonsensical dream for once in my life?  Then again, I like plots.  What can I say?  It goes with my love of pens and paper.

For a little clarity about what's been going on in my family, it's my dad and his brothers.  And their families.  My grandmother, you see, is reaching the age of 88 and still lives alone in the house and home she built with her husband.  He's long since deceased, and she's starting to have trouble living alone.  But she doesn't relaly want to move.  And decisions were being made without everyones consent, and namecalling ensued, and personal attacks, and things that I'm ashamed to say happened within a family that I thought was anything but what they now appear to be.  My parents took the best road they could instead.  My mom moved up north to live with my Grandmother for 6 months... and she's just the daughter in law!  It has quieted everyone else for a time, but she's deeply hurt by what some people were saying before all of this of her and my father.  To see your uncles and aunts reduced to preschoolers in your eyes just like that... is painful to say the least.  But I guess they're human just like all of us.  And I do understand that these decisions are hard ones.  It's their mother they're discussing.  And her limited future.  But there comes a time when you have to say  to hell with what we need.  What does 'SHE' need.

It's supposed to be about my Grandmother.  Not about how they want to act before they go to Florida this year.  For the love of God... I thought they were better than this.

Anyway, I'm now pretty vented, and tired.  I want to go to bed.  I want to dream something a little more freeing than what I've been dreaming.  Maybe I'll fly tonight.  Just take a look at everything from high up.  Everything looks like it works so well together when you're that high up.  The greens, and blues.  The rivers taking the paths of least resistance, the mountains growing tall and then small.  And then tall again.  The oceans and forests.  At least, it looks like that in my dreams.  No Great Wall, no Pyramids.  Just greens and blues, and clouds too.  That's where I want to go tonight.

Someone once told me that I might start to become jaded.  I don't want to go that way.  It was another pisces who said it.  He himself had become so jaded as to have no trust of anyone.  And it pained me to see.  I don't want that to happen.  That's not the kind of world I live in.  That isn't what I see most of the time.  I just hope I'm not being naieve.  I truly want to believe.

With love, to all of you.  Because I can and do.  Because it's the only thing that keeps me going.

Shane

[Posted 10/21/2004 at 11:35 PM]

=== Monday October 11, 2004 ===

There's so much I want to write right now.  So much crap that's apparently happening in and around my family.  The 'Rock' that I perceived to be the 'Fera family' all my life is somehow crumbling.  How the hell is it that people up to 40 years my senior can be so goddamn childish?  It makes me sick, and makes me sad, and makes me so many damn things I don't know how to write it all down.  All my life I've seen my family, I've learned about actions and consequence.  About honesty, integrity, and love.  About family and bonds.  All my life I've developed a belief in altruism.  That we're altruistic at heart, and I just don't know anymore.

And I'm sure there'll be a line outside my door one day of people mouthing the words 'I told you so'.  The people that my optimism could never get to.  The ones that left my life by their own choices.

Why isn't it all the way I've percieved it in my head all my life?  What has happened to people?  Lordy... I'm certain that I'll go crazy before I die in life.  That much I'm fairly certain of.  Because it'll be the only way I could possibly come to terms with the way reality seems to be.

Most of what I write starts with 'we this' or 'most of us that'.  But what I need to start doing is writing with the word 'I' in front of my paragraphs.  I need to take ownership of my own beliefs, dreams, and wants.  While there may be people out there that feel the same with some of what I say, I need to stop speaking for them right off the bat.

I am me.  There are many things that I believe, but there are many things that are a little fuzzy these days.  I am going to put some of my beliefs down on paper.  Because I need them there.  Frankly, I just need to write tonight.  A mental and emotional purging.  I just need to.

+++

I believe in God.  Or that Greater Being.  Or, whatever you choose to call it.  The totality of all existence.  I just do.  I believe.
I want to find love.  I want to feel that connection again.  I want to be loved at the same time I'm loving someone.  I've had that before, but by my own choices I sent it away.  That's a goal.  I need a kindred spirit to marry, or someone who doesn't care about all the things that may mark me eccentric to some.  I believe in experiencing life.  I love to run my hands over bark.  I love to smell the rain.  I love to feel sand between my toes, and I love to feel gravel beneath my bare feet.  I love the feeling of water slowly creeping over my skin.  Rising to cover all of me.  I love holding my breath under the water until I can't hold it any more.  I love to just float face down in the water, while my mind floats away elsewhere.
I love passion.  Candles.  Music.  Writing.  Photography.  And beauty,  but since I see so damn many things as beautiful that's kind of like saying I like to breathe.  I also like computer games.  I like reading.  I like riding my bike.  I love animals, and sometimes talk to chipmunks.  I drink loudly, not slirpy, but somehow slightly louder than normal I guess.  I'm a little hard of hearing, but I need to check that out.
I believe in life.  I believe that nobody has the right to take another's life.  It's just what I believe. I don't really want to argue about it, it's just my belief.  It seems hipocritical to me to end someone's life to show people not to end others lives.
I believe that everyone matters.  You matter.  I matter.  We all matter!  And I desperately want to believe again that we are all altruistic at heart.
I love old books.  The smell, the memories they contain.  Not my own, but you know someone's memories are stored within.
I'm in love with emotion.  I love feeling.  I love that I can feel emotion.  I think it's a wonderful gift that we can feel emotion, and I think it's also a curse.
I believe I'm tired just now and want to sleep.  I also believe that's where I'm going to go.  I have so many thoughts going through my head right now, and I don't think I'm even typing in any kind of paragraphs or in any organized sort of way.

I guess I'm just off the wall tonight.  Watching movies does that to me.  And so does certain information.  I promise I will write about what contributed to my writing like crazy here tonight, but that's for another time.  I need to sleep now.

I want to wish you all a very happy thanksgiving.  Canadian Thanksgiving that is.  And I'd like to give thanks tonight.  For life.  For family.  And for true friends.  And for the love I'll one day find.  She's out there, I'm sure of it.  Probably writing like crazy herself somewhere.  Because I figure the only way that any significant other will accept me in the future, is if she too sometimes finds herself thinking just a little too much about important things and unimportant things alike.

Hey, this is life.  I'm going to live it one day and night at a time.

Peace to you,

Shane

[Posted 10/11/2004 at 1:29 AM]

=== Wednesday October 6, 2004 ===

The Marriage of True Minds (Poem 20)

For you, as I now rest tonight,
my energy is yours; that's right,
all yours as my eyes shut in dreams
peruse my thoughts, from seam to seams

My energy, yours now to wield
for charging lance, or just raised shield
I do not need it as I sleep
For I above in heaven creep

And when you lay you down to rest,
I hope your own will be my vest
while I charge day ahead full force
To lend me strength to stay my course.

Our marriage one of ever changing tides,
A love that never ever shall pick sides.

+++

Shane

=== Tuesday October 5, 2004 ===

Used to Be (Poem 19)

I was 16 once,
writing my first poem
to speak for me

I never had the guts to say
everything that passed
from thought to dream
from dream to
distant longing

Only in words did strength find me
and drive me to those acts
only ever imagined
hugging notebooks to my chest

acting in plays and musicals
to pretend to be elsewise
even for a little while

so when words fail me
I feel so lost
and I'm 16 again, wearing masks
trying to be sane, and normal
in this very abnormal day and age
where words are everywhere
and voices hard to find

+++

Shane

[Posted 10/5/2004 at 10:44 PM]

=== Monday October 4, 2004 ===

Memory

You're everything I wanted in a memory,
Pristine, perfect,
You compell me.
You are. My mind cannot refute.
Your memory is far clearer
than those realities were ever lived.

I regret all those things
my memory slips into my head.

Your memory forgives, but mine...
my memory lingers on your voice
your smile and your laughter in the air.

You're everything I wanted in a memory,
but I'm relentless,
and it never fits the way I want it to.
So I'm compelled to remember each moment
again, and again, and again,
Until even my memories find end.

+++

Shane
[Posted 10/4/2004 at 11:6 PM]

=== Sunday October 3, 2004 ===

Colouring Seven (Poem 16)

I'm past the point
where movies all about my life
make me twist inside

I never lived my life
they never let me out.

I never got the bubble
between the lines
and couldn't get my colour
to stay there either.

On rocky ground,
a house of glass

all the better to see me with
and the better to see out from
behind a camera
I get to see it all.

A stranger to the street
the steady pace beneath my feet
never wanted constancy
just a little love, you see

but I never could keep my bubble
between those two damn lines
and I never figured much would come
from going back and forth
to get it absolutely on

I'd rather burn away
than spend my waking time
adjusting constantly
to changing lines
that were never mine.

I never could colour in-between,
but they never let me out

+++

Shane

(There's something here, but what I cannot tell. I'ts far from done, but damn, I'd swear there's something here. I'm too tired to see it right now. So I'll leave it as it. Peace.)

=== Saturday October 2, 2004 ===

Gritty Mirrors Never Lie (Poem 15)

I'd like it to be about
everything else for a change
the unmentionables,
the undesirables,
the things that remain with us
stored away in glad-bags
or tupperware.

Shown never,
ashamed of a voice
that is our own,
but long past changed.

Even perfection goes bad,
and perfection we never quite are,
but perfect all the same
in our acceptance of that.

We are the tupperware,
the glad-bags,
closet-hidden things.

We are the footsteps in the sand
the crap that floats on top
of the cleanest water

we are

and we are perfect
in that imperfection
that's clarity like no other
a soluble insolubility

the choice never made,
but taken all the same.

+++

Shane

[Posted 10/2/2004 at 2:28 AM]

=== Monday November 29, 2004 ===

A Lullabye to Tomorrow

My internet has been down for a week or so, hence the lack of many posts except from work and other computers.  I've been both inspired to write, as well as inspired to sleep, frequently in the past week and weekend.  That being said, the inspiration to sleep has been the stronger of the two until now, and even still I find myself unable to write effectively, or for very long without my eyes slipping closed and sending me to that place enchanted and haunted.  Where you exist in full form.  Not just as memory, or dream, or wish.  Where you sparkle far more brightly than Venus before dawn.  But knowing that the dream, and wish, and memory are all I'm left with come sunrise... it's enough to hold on to what I can when I can, and how I can.

You may be my inspiration, but you have many names, and many forms.  You may spark genius and stupidity both in the same night, causing me to fumble over my words which I imagined to be much more lucid or vivid.  My words fail me when you arrive.  My words, my strength, my aptitude for anything fails me when I see your eyes.  I become more concious of my breath than ever before.  Stuck in my throat, my whispered words rising slowly and without destination.  A ramble... an amble!  A river of meaningless words instead of the meaning within their tangled verse.  You see through that, I think, but it's meaningless as my mind cannot grasp such simple truths in your presence.

I melt.  And in that melting become everything all at once, but nothing I think you can pinpoint.  And that's my error.  That's my own fault.  I fade away with far more passion than I should, when dancing right in front of you is all I want.  Your eyes straight to my eyes is all I need.  Sometimes I believe if our souls were to meet where our eyes touch each other, that they would realize their error and never separate again.  And the world would weep to lose us in each other.  And it almost wouldn't matter.  So I wait.  I wait for such a time when our eyes can tango.

Till then, sweet dreams,Shane

[Posted 11/29/2004 at 1:25 AM]

=== Wednesday November 24, 2004 ===

Fruit of the Gods

The pomegranate is the most perfect fruit, I think.  It's my favourite fruit.  I swear it's ambrosia.  I swear there's a little piece of the afterlife in every bite.  It's texture, taste, colour, all in one.  I just wanted to share that, after having eaten through one just now.  I first had a pomegranate when I was in University.  It was love at first bite.  Though it took me more than a few trips to pick some up before I perfected (nearly) the art of eating one.  They can be tricky, and never wear white.  The purple colouring of the inner-parts stain like a sonnofabitch.  But, if you've never had one before, I reccomend having one.  Highly.  If you need help in the eating, let me know, but share one with your loved ones, friends, family, strangers on the street.

Pomegranates: making crazy people rave on about them since I first started raving on about them.

Peace,Shane

[Posted 11/24/2004 at 1:0 AM]
